21a7(phal chen): rgyas la mchod pa dang / rim gro mngon par 'du byab pa de dag sems bskyed pa gcig gis mngon par 'du byed la/ tshul de lta bur sems bskyed pa re rer mnyes par byed pas/ shar phyog logs su 'jig rten gyi khams tshad med par
21b1(phal chen): gtogs pa'i sems can rnams dang lhan cig pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das tshad med pa mnyes par byas te/ gzhung de bzhin du thog ma la ji skad du brjod pa de bzhin du gnyis pa la dpag tu med pa/ gsum pa la grangs
21b2(phal chen): med pa/ bzhi pa la bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ lnga pa la mtshungs pa med pa/ drug pa la kun tu mtha' yas pa/ bdun pa la mu med pa/ brgyad pa la sa mtshams med pa/ dgu pa la gzhal du med pa'i bar du ste/
21b3(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dpe snga ma de dag lta'ang zhog gi/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di la skyes bu bcu pa zhig skye ste/ skyes bu snga ma dgu po de dag dang / 'jig rten gyi khams gzhal du med pa bcur gtogs pa'i sems can
21b4(phal chen): pha la de dag gis bskal pa dpag tu med par sangs rgyas mchod pa dang / rim gros mnyes par byas pa de tsam du sems bskyed pa gcig gis mnyes par byed cing / tshul de ltar sems bskyed pa re rer mnyes
21b5(phal chen): par byed pas/ shar phyogs logs su 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med par gtogs pa'i sems can rnams dang lhan cig pas zhal zas bro ba'i mchog brjod du med pa zhes bya ba nas/ gzhan yang rgya cher te/
21b6(phal chen): de lta bus sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das brjod du med pa mnyes par byas pa nas/ kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' sems dang po bskyed pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po la bskal pa brjod du med par gtogs
21b7(phal chen): pa'i sangs rgyas mchod pa dang / bsnyen bkur ba las byung ba'i bsod nams kyi phung po snga mas brgya'i char yang nye bar mi 'gro zhes bya ba nas/ rgyu'i bar du yang nye bar mi 'gro zhes bya ba'i bar du ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/
22a1(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras de ni 'di ltar sangs rgyas skyes pa de tsam nyi tshe zhig mchod cing bsnyen bkur ba 'am/ sangs rgyas kyi mchod pa'i yo byad de tsam dag gi phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
22a2(phal chen): chen po rnams bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems mi skye'i/ de ni 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa ma lus pa thams cad chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas
22a3(phal chen): gtugs pa/ brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa/ phyogs bcu tshad las 'das pa/ 'byam klas pa/ phyogs bcu'i rnam grangs mtha' yas pa'i dra bas khyab pa/ mig 'phrul gyi rnam pas bsam yas pa/ 'jig rten gyi
22a4(phal chen): khams thams cad gzhi mnyam par chud pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus par 'dus pa'i tshul shin tu bstan pa/ 'du shes kyi rnam pa la gnas pa'i phyogs kyi dra ba rnam par phye ba la gnas pa thams cad du gtogs pa/
22a5(phal chen): lhag ma med par ma lus pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi grangs dang tshul shin tu bstan pa dag tu sngon gyi mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa bgrangs pa'i tshul shin tu bstan par gtogs pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi
22a6(phal chen): tshul gyis mngon par thugs su chud pa dag tu/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang ji snyed nub par gyur te/ yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa dang / gang yang ma 'ongs pa'i dus na/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin
22a7(phal chen): gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams 'byung bar 'gyur ba dang / gang yang da ltar byung ba'i dus na/ da ltar phyogs bcu na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams bzhugs shing 'tsho
22b1(phal chen): gzhes pa dang / chos ston pa de dag thams cad mchod cing rim gro bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems skye ste/ sems bskyed pa de skyes ma zag nas
22b2(phal chen): de dang der 'das pa'i grangs su gtogs pa sngon gyi mur gyur pa ji snyed pa de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gis mngon par thugs su chud pa de dag tu/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang ji snyed mya ngan las 'das pa de dag gi
22b3(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba ji lta ba bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yid ches so/ / de bzhin gshegs pa ma byon pa de dang de'i dus su gtogs pa phyi ma'i mtha'i mur bstan pa/ dpag tu med pa mtha' dang dbus med
22b4(phal chen): par shin tu bstan pa dag tu/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang ji snyed 'byung bar 'gyur pa de dag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba la yang byang chub sems dpa' de yid ches so// da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin
22b5(phal chen): gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ye shes mtha' dang dbus med par bstan pa/ ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba la yang byang chub sems dpa'
22b6(phal chen): de yid ches shing yongs su 'dzin par byed/ yongs su rgyas par byed/ rab tu 'thob par byed/ khong du chud par byed/ rab tu rig par byed/ shin tu sgrub par byed/ rgyud gcig tu
22b7(phal chen): gyur par byed/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyang mnyam pa nyid du khong du chud par byed do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar sems bskyed pa de ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gdung rgyun mi
23a1(phal chen): 'chad pa'i phyir skye'o/ / 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rgyas par dgang ba'i phyir skye'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gtogs pa'i
23a2(phal chen): sems can yongs su bsgral ba'i phyir skye'o/ / 'jig rten gyi khams tha ma cad du 'du ba dang 'jig pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gtogs pa'i
23a3(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi srid pa gsum yongs su dag pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir
23a4(phal chen): skye'o/ / sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / bag la nyal ba dang / bag chags thams cad yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye'o// sems can thams cad kyi shi 'pho dang skye ba yongs su shes
23a5(phal chen): par bya ba'i phyir skye'o/ / sems can thams cad kyi dbang po dang sbyor ba yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye'o// sems can thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye'o// sems
23a6(phal chen): can thams cad kyi dus gsum gyi shes pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir skye ste/ sems bskyed pa des sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dag dang nye bar 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ma byon
23a7(phal chen): padang da ltar byang ba rnams dang nye bar 'gyur ro/ / 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu nye bar 'gro'o// mabyon pa dang nga ltar byang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu nye bar 'gro'o// sangs rgyas bcom
23b1(phal chen): ldan 'das 'das nas kyi chos kyang thob par 'gyur ro/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ma byon pa rnams kyi chos kyang thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das da ltar byung ba rnams kyi chos car
23b2(phal chen): thob par 'gyur ro/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa rnams dang mnyam pa nyid du nye bar 'gro'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba rnams dang mnyam pa nyid du nye bar
23b3(phal chen): 'gro'o/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa rnams kyi ye shes kyi tshogs rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ma byon pa dang da ltar byang ba rnams kyi ye shes kyi tshogs kyang
23b4(phal chen): rnam par dag par 'gyur ro/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang / sa byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i stobs la thub pa med pa shin tu brtan par 'gyur ro// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang /
23b5(phal chen): da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dag gi mi bsnyengs pa yongs su dag pa'ang yongs su rdzogs par byed do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa rnams kyi bstan par bya ba'i sangs rgyas kyi
23b6(phal chen): chos kyi rgyan mnyam pa nyid kyang rjes su 'thob bo/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba rnams kyi bstan par bya ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi rkyen mnyam pa nyid kyang yongs su rdzogs par
23b7(phal chen): byed do/ / nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa chos kyi dbyings kyi mtha' dang dbus med par shin tu bstan pa'i dus gsum mnyam pa nyid du thugs su chung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyang rjes su 'thob
24a1(phal chen): po/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ltar de ni sangs rgyas su shog cig ces bya ba'i sems bskyed pa des/ 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang nye ba yin/ ma byon
24a2(phal chen): pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang nye ba yin/ 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi yul rnams dang mnyam pa yin// 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi
24a3(phal chen): chos rnams dang mnyam pa yin no/ / ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams dang mnyam pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi yul thams cad dang mnyam pa yin/ gcig tu nges pa'i lus gcig tu
24a4(phal chen): gyur pas kyang / dus gsum du mnyam pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes dang 'grogs pa yang thob ste/ ye shes de dang 'grogs par gyur pa'i sems bskyed pa byung ba de skyes ma thag tu
24a5(phal chen): phyogs bcu na sangs rgyas rnams kyang ched du brjod pa mdzad do/ / sems bskyed pa de nyid rten du mdzad de/ bdul ba ji bzhin du chos kyang yang dag par ston/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
24a6(phal chen): du'ang 'dul ba tshad med pa rnams 'byung bar 'gyur/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyang rab tu g.yo bar 'gyur/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyang snang bas rgyas par 'gyur/ 'jig rten
24a7(phal chen): gyi khams thams cad kyi ngan song yang rgyun chad par 'gyur/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyang yongs su dag par 'gyur/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du sangs rgyas 'byung ba yang yang dag
24b1(phal chen): par ston par 'gyur/ sems can thams cad kyang rab tu dga' bar 'gyur/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad la yang rab tu 'jug par 'gyur/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs thams cad kyang yongs su
24b2(phal chen): 'dzin par 'gyur/ sangs rgyas kyi rig kyi snang ba thams cad kyang rab tu thob par 'gyur te/ dus gsum du gtogs pa la sems bskyed pa der sangs rgyas sam sangs rgyas kyi chos sam
24b3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' 'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i chos sam/ rang sangs rgyas sam/ rang sangs rgyas kyi chos sam/ nyan thos sam/ nyan thos kyi chos sam/ 'jig
24b4(phal chen): rten pa 'am/ 'jig rten pa'i chos sam/ 'jig rten las 'das pa 'am/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos sam/ sems can nam/ sems can gyi chos kyang rung ste/
24b5(phal chen): ma 'dus pa gang yang med de/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni ma gtogs so// de ltar na sems bskyed pa der ni chos kyi dbyings thams cad 'dus so// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus de'i tshe/
24b6(phal chen): phyogs bcur 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rnam pa drug tu g.yos par gyur te/ g.yos so// rab tu g.yos so// kun tu g.yos so// 'gul to//
24b7(phal chen): rab tu 'gul to// kun tu 'gul to// ldeg go// rab tu ldeg go// kun tu ldeg go// che ma ches/ rab tu chem chem/ kun tu chem chem mo// 'ur 'ur/ rab tu 'u mthar
25a1(phal chen): kun tu 'ur 'ur ro/ / shig shig/ rab tu shig shig/ kun tu shig shig go// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / sems bskyed pa de'i yon tan yang dag par brjod
25a2(phal chen): pa'i chos nyid rab tu thob pa'i phyir/ lha rdzas kyi me tog gi char yang mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi spos kyi char yang mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi phye ma'i char yang mngon par bab po//
25a3(phal chen): lha rdzas kyi 'phreng ba'i char yang mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi gos kyi char yang mngon pa rabab bo// lha rdzas kyi rin po che'i char yang mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi rgyan gyi char yang mngon par
25a4(phal chen): bab bo/ / lha rdzas kyi rol mo rnams kyang mngon par sgra 'byin par gyur to// lha rdzas kyi snang ba yang rab tubyung ngo // lha rdzas kyi 'od kyang rab tu byung ngo // phyogs bcur 'jig rten gyi khams
25a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa'i pha rol nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi blo gros su mtshan btags pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis zhal mngon par
25a6(phal chen): bstan te gsung brjod pa/ chos kyi blo gros legs so legs so// phyogs bcu na de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis chos bstan pa de la ched du brjod pa mdzad
25a7(phal chen): ngo/ / nged kyis kyang chos bstan pa 'di nyid shin tu rnam par phye ste/ nged kyis ji ltar shin tu rnam par phye ba de bzhin du/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis kyang shin tu rnam par phye'o// 'di nyid du
25b1(phal chen): / yang khyod kyi chos bstan pa des byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis byang chub tu sems bskyed do// de dag kyang nged kyis lung bstan te/ de dag ni ma
25b2(phal chen): 'ongs pa'i dus bskal pa stong phrag brjod du med pa'i mthar thams cad kyang dus gcig tu 'jig rten gyi khams ming tha dad pa dag tu/ de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan gcig pa sha stag 'byung bar 'gyur
25b3(phal chen): 'di ltar sems rnam par dag pa zhes bya ba sha stag tu 'gyur ro/ / nged kyis chos bstan pa 'di yang ji ltar ma 'ongs pa'i dus na/ ma 'ongs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ma thos pa rnams
25b4(phal chen): kyis thos par bya ba dang / ji ltar 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed 'dir sems can rnams kyis shes shing gleng bzhi pa 'di'i ri rab kyi rtse mo la ji ltar sems can rnams 'dul bar gyur pa de bzhin du
25b5(phal chen): phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi kham bye ba pa khrag khrig brgya stong tshad med pa/ grangs med pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ mtshungs pa med pa/ kun tu mtha' yas pa/ dpag tu med pa
25b6(phal chen): sa mtshams med pa/ brjod du med pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ nam mkha'i mthas gtugs pa dag tu yang / sems can rnams 'dul bar 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir byin gyis
25b7(phal chen): brlab bo/ / thams cad na yang chos bstan pa 'di nyid byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros shes bya ba sha stag sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi sngon gyi smon lam gyis sangs rgyas kyi
26a1(phal chen): chos thams cad yang dag par bstan pa dang / ye shes kyi snang ba shin tu gsal bar bya ba dang / don gyis gdul ba'i ltung ba thob pa dang / chos nyid rab tu 'thob par byas/
26a2(phal chen): dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnam pa shin tu dga' bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi rgyu yang dag par bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos mnyam pa nyid du bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings
26a3(phal chen): gnyis su med pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir rab tu ston to/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros kyis phyogs bcur bltas te/ 'khor thams cad la rnam par bsdus nas
26a4(phal chen): nam mkha'i khams la ni rnam par spyod/ / sems can gyi khams ni yongs su smin par byed/ las dang rnam par smin pa'i khams ni'i gal bar mi byed/ nam mkha'i khams ni yongs su dag
26a5(phal chen): par byed/ kun nas nyon mongs pa las byung ba ni rab tu sel/ mos pa yangs pa las byung ba ni shin tu 'phel bar byed/ sems can gyi dbang po tha dad pa la ni rab tu 'jug/ dus gsum ni
26a6(phal chen): mnyam par byed/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings la ni yang dag par rtog cing / rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i stobs yongs su dag par bya ba la gzhol ba'i phyir/ de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi mthus tshigs
26a7(phal chen): su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ / gang zhig phyogs rnams bcu po ma lus rgyas byas shing // sems can zhing dang chos gsum dag kyang rtogs gyur pa// sangs rgyas mtsho mchog byang chub sems dpa'
26b1(phal chen): de bzhin te/ / de dag 'jig rten phan phyir sems kyi dam pa skyed// nam mkha'i dbyings kyis klas pa'i chos dbyings ji bzhin dang // ji ltar sangs rgyas chos rnams 'gro kun rjes song dang /
26b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kun tu khyab brnyes ji bzhin gyi// 'gro ba mi ldog don du phan par rab tu zhugs// 'jig rten rnams la byams pas rtag par rab gnas shing // 'tshe ba med par 'gro la
26b3(phal chen): phan phyir su zhugs te/ / snang ba ma zer 'od byed gnas su gyur pa'i rnams// bsam gyis mi khyab stobs bcu mnga' bas byin gyis brlabs// de ni zhing rnams tha dad pa yin tshul yang rnyed
26b4(phal chen): de ni lus kyi rnam pa kun la rab tu zhugs/ / bsod nams ye shes de yang sangs rgyas byang chub bzhin// de ni chags med gzhol ba ye shes rgyur skyes so// spri'u tshugs rgyu ba'i 'gro ba sna tshogs
26b5(phal chen): ma lus par/ / gzhan yang zhing rnams 'byam klas chags med mthar thug pa// de dag phra sbom rgya che yangs pa thams cad du// byang chub sems mchog de ni gcig pu kun tu 'gro// brjod
26b6(phal chen): du med pa shin tu phra zhing mi gnas pa'i/ / byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa'i mchog la rtag zhugs shing // mkhas pa gang gis sangs rgyas chos mthong mi ngoms pa// de dag chos rnams rgya mtsho'i rnam
26b7(phal chen): par chud pa yin/ / 'jig rten lam rgyud kun la su zhig snying brtse zhing // 'jig rten gsum po sbyang bar rtag tu zhugs pa'i rnams// phyi ma'i mthar thug sangs rgyas gdung gi rgyun mi gcod//
27a1(phal chen): de ni bdud kyi khyim yang rab tu 'joms pa yin// dus gsum rgyal ba rnams dang rgyud gcig dngos gyur cing // shin tu phra ba'i tshul gyis lam la rtag brtson te// su zhig
27a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas yul la dang sems pa/ / de ni tshigs med thub pa kun gyis dbang yang bskur// rdo rje lta bur sra zhing brtan la mi shigs pa// rkang gnyis gtso bos mdzad pa rtag tu dran shes shing //
27a3(phal chen): 'dren pa'i spyod yul snang rab shin tu rnyed pa'i rnams// gzhan gyi dri nga la mi rgyug byang chub sems kyang skye// 'gro ba rnams kyi 'du shes rnam pa mang shes shing // de bzhin las dang 'bras bu
27a4(phal chen): sems kyi rnams kyang ste/ / gzhan yang dbang po'i mthu dang khams rnams du ma dag/ kun kyang byang chub sems la spyod yul gcig yin no// gang zhig chos kyi dbyings bzhin byang chub sems
27a5(phal chen): yangs shing / / rtag tu chos la mi gnas nam mkha' ji bzhin pa// chags med sems ldan de dag sangs rgyas ye shes zhugs// de dag rtog med chos can yang dag mtha' la gnas//
27a6(phal chen): sems can bsas pa rnam 'byed sems can 'du shes med// chos kyi nam rtog khrag khrig pa mthar rab tu phyin// de dag rtog la mos shing rnam par mi rtog ste// de dag zhing rnams bye ba khrag
27a7(phal chen): khrig rjes su zhugs/ / gang zhig sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig rjes sems shing // gang zhig chos dbyings tshul gyi mdzod du zhugs gyur la// gang zhig sems can dbang po'i rnam par
27b1(phal chen): / mthar phyin pa// de dag sems can gtso bzhin chos nyid shes pa yin// lhag pa'i bsam pa dge dang rtag par mngon ldan zhing // skyes bu'i seng ge'i bsnyen bkur phyir ldog mi 'gyur la/
27b2(phal chen): 'jig rten gtso bos mkhas pa zong bas mi ngoms pa// de dag sangs rgyas khrag khrig bye bas byin gyis brlabs// zab mo'i chos rnams rnam par 'byed kyang chags pa med // gnas pa med
27b3(phal chen): pas sems kyi dam pa rtag tu dag/ de dag bskal pa mtha' yas skyes bu seng ge'i sems// dus gsum chags pa med par rtogs pa'i yid dang ldan// mi phrogs thub par mi nus yid kyi
27b4(phal chen): dbang po dang / / gsum pa rjes su song dang rtag tu ldan gyur cing // chos rnams 'byam klas shin tu bslabs pas rmongs med pa// de dag chos dbyings 'gengs kyang nam yang mi ngoms
27b5(phal chen): so/ / tshig gi lam 'das ji bzhin mkhas pa zhi ba shes// de bzhin nyid la nam yang rnam par mi 'byed pa// de dag sangs rgyas thams cad yul la rjes sems shing // dus gsum
27b6(phal chen): chags pa med pa rtogs pa'i yi de ldan 'gyur/ / mkhas pa gang zhig sems bskyed 'byam klas chos kyi dbyings// 'gengs shing phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas zhing du 'gro ba ni/ de dag khrag
27b7(phal chen): khrig tshul rnams brjod du med pa yi/ / snang ba rnyed par gnas pa'i rgyal ba'i sras yin no// chos rab mu stegs snying rje'o tshul gyi rjes song zhing // byams pa'i pha rol phyin pa bar snang rdzi
28a1(phal chen): bzhin te/ / sems can khams la rnams kyang yongs su rtog med pa// de dag rnam rtog med la brtson zhing 'jig rten spyod// phyogs bcu dag tu bden pas 'gro ba yid
28a2(phal chen): 'bebs par/ / 'dong bas sems can gtso bo de dag kun tu rgyu// bden pa'i tshig brtson rtag tu nges pa'i sems ldan pa// de dag phyogs bcu'i mi yi mchog gis byin gyis brlabs//
28a3(phal chen): 'das par gyur pa'i dus kyang de dag rjes su dran// de bzhin ma 'ongs dus na 'jug pa rnam par bsgom// de dag phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten kun na mi gnas te// sems can phan dang dgrol
28a4(phal chen): phyir kun tu rnam par rgyu/ / ye shes 'od mchog dam pas chags pa med gyur pa// rgyu yi rnam pa chos rab nem nur med brtan rnams// de dag the tshom thams cad rnam par zlog pa byed//
28a5(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings 'dir nam nur med par rab tu 'jug/ gang zhig bdud rnams kun gyi gnas rnams 'joms byed dang // gang yang sems can rab ribi shin tu se la byed dang // gang rnams
28a6(phal chen): rtog pa 'jig cing rnam rtog mi 'grogs pa/ / sems can gtso bo de dag yul la the tshom med// dus gsum ma lus the tshom rnam par bzlog byas shing // bsam pa mchog gis de bzhin
28a7(phal chen): gshegs pa'i drung 'gro ste/ / dad pa'i stobs dang ldan zhing blo brtan rnyed pa'i rnams// de dag don rtogs khong du chud cing blo yang dag/ mkhas pa 'gro ba'i don du phyi ma'i mthar spro ste/
28b1(phal chen): sems can don du rnam thar 'byam klas yongs su tshol// yun ring dus su skyo ba med cing zhum pa med// sems can dmyal ba sdug bsngal mang po zlog par byed// de dag bsod nams mi
28b2(phal chen): zad ye shes ldan/ / 'gro ba'i dbang po sna tshogs bsam la rab tu 'jug/ skye dgu'i las kyi rgyud kyang shin tu shes byas shing // bsam pa ji bzhin tshul 'dra'i chos rnams mtha' yas
28b3(phal chen): brjod/ / 'gro la byams pa'i sa rnams kun dang rjes su ldan// bdag med nyid rtogs 'on kyang btang snyoms byed pa min// de dag snying brtse gcig tu gsal bar chos kyang brjod//
28b4(phal chen): 'on kyang dmigs par mi gnas de dag 'jig rten rgyu// de dag 'od zer dra ba sna tshogs mdog bkye zhing // 'gro ba'i mun pa bsal te kun tu snang byas nas// 'od zer sgo yi pad+mo dag la
28b5(phal chen): rgyal sras rnams/ / kun tu bstan te rdul dang bral ba'i chos kyang sngon// spu gcig rtse la zhing rnams rgyal bas brgyan pa dang // de bzhin rgyal ba'i sras kyis brgyan pa mngon par mthong
28b6(phal chen): 'khor rnams blo sems gzhan dang gzhan can dpe med pa/ / 'gro ba de dag sems shes rmongs med ston pa byed// sems 'jug gcig gis phyogs rnams bcu po thams cad kyi//
28b7(phal chen): brjod du med pa khrag khrig zhing rnams kun bgrod cing // song ste sangs rgyas 'gro ba'i don du mchod byas nas// dri ba khrag khrig don dang ldan pa sna tshogs 'dri// bde gshegs rnams la pha
29a1(phal chen): yi 'du shes nyer bzhag cing / / chos kyi gter mkhas rtag tu shes rab non po can// ye shes 'byung gnas mkhas pas sangs rgyas chags med phyir// 'gro ba'i don
29a2(phal chen): 'dod byang chub mchog gi spyod pa sgrub/ / gang rnams chos dbyings rnam par phye zhing bsas byas kyang // bskal pa mang po 'das byas pad par ma gyur te// chos nyid gnas med gang la'ang chud par
29a3(phal chen): mgyur kyang / / chags med ye shes can rnams skyo sem med par spyod// dus gsum rgyal ba'i rigs su rigs dang ldan gyur cing // bde gshegs kun gyi sku las yang dag byang gyur pas/
29a4(phal chen): chos kyi lus can de dag 'gro la gzugs lus ston// sgyu mkhon mkhas pa yid 'ong sgyu ma ston pa bzhin// mkhas pa de dag la lar spyod pa mchog rnyed snang // la lar mkhas pa skye
29a5(phal chen): zhing mya ngan 'das par snang / / byang chub dam pa'i mchog kyang rnam par 'tshang rgya snang // mya ngan 'da' ba ston pa'ang de bzhin la lar snang // rang rgyal rnams dang nyan thos rgyal ba'i sa min pa'o//
29a6(phal chen): chos nyid de la ji ltar rab tu gnas pa ltos// lus dang sgra med pas ma med 'du shes ldan pa min// 'on kyang bya ba sna tshogs du mnye bar ston// 'gro bar chos rnams rnam par 'byed cing skyer
29a7(phal chen): 'gyur te/ / 'jig rten gtso bo mi bzhugs phyin rgyal sras rnams/ chags med mthar phyin pa yi ye shes gnas bcas te// sangs rgyas byin rlabs rnam par 'phrul pa dag kyang ston/
29b1(phal chen): 'jig rten 'di na de dag 'dra ba gang yang med// de dag pas kyang 'phags pa lta go ci zhig smos// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yangs pa ma thob par// thams cad mkhyen pa'i thabs su rnam
29b2(phal chen): 'phrul mchog kyang thob/ / gang rnams chos rab 'phags par rtag tu 'jug byed pa// de dag chos rab dam pa mchog gi theg pa yin// 'jig rten dus dang dus min tshod kyang shes byas shing //
29b3(phal chen): de dag 'gro la phan phyir rnam par 'phrul pa ston// dpa' ba gang rnams zhing kun bdag gi lus 'gengs shing // gang rnams 'jig rten 'od zer dra ba mchog gtong ba// mun pa bsal cing snang bas 'jig
29b4(phal chen): rten rgyas par byed/ / klu yi dbang po bzhin du chos kyi char pa 'bebs// rmi lam lta bu log pa'i sgyu ma 'dra ba yi// 'du byed rab tu shes nas lam rnams sbyor 'jug cing // 'gro ba thams cad
29b5(phal chen): snying rje chen pos khyab byas nas/ / rang bzhin dag pa thar lam bya ba med pa ston// gang rnams rgyal ba'i stobs rnams ji bzhin tshad med dang // gang rnams mkha' ltar 'gro ba kun tu mtha' yas shing //
29b6(phal chen): gang rnams sems can khams kun yongs su dgrol brtson pa// de dag bskal pa bye ba grangs med spyad pa spyod// las mchog bla na med pa shin tu sbyangs pa yis// yon tan dam pa sna tshogs rnams
29b7(phal chen): kyang kun sems shing / byang chub sems dpa' de dag spyod pa mchog mi mthong // thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes 'byung ba rnam par lta// sems 'byung gcig gis 'jig rten bsam gyis
30a1(phal chen): mi khyab pa/ / 'byam klas kun tu rgyu zhing 'gro bar rab tu snang // rtog dang rnam rtog mi 'byed dag pa'i sems dang ldan// de dag gcig min lus la lus gcig ston pa byed/
30a2(phal chen): de dag 'jig rten kun la rtog par mi byed de// mgon po kun gyi chos nyid yongs su mi rtog go// de dag chos kun rnam 'byed 'dod chags bral gyur kyang // 'gro ba thar bar bya ba yongs su mi gtong
30a3(phal chen): ngongo/ / 'jig rten kun gyi 'du shes rnam pa gang yod pa// bzang ngan 'bring dang de bzhin chung dang sna tshogs kyi// 'du shes thibs po dag dang rab rgal rnam phye ste// de dag byin brlabs rnam par
30a4(phal chen): 'phrul ba shin tu ston/ / ji ltar sgyu ma rnam pa sna tshogs tshad med pa// de 'dra'i rnam par 'phrul pas chos dbyings 'di dag 'gengs// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas lus kyi bye brag gis//
30a5(phal chen): 'gro ba rnams kyi mos pa ji bzhin ston pa byed// de dag gang la'angam chags rtog dang rnam rtog med// dog pa med cing nyon mongs de bzhin rlom sems med// de dag sangs rgyas chags pa'i blo med
30a6(phal chen): tha ra la min/ / 'gro ba kun la'ang bde ba'i 'du shes rab tu skyed// 'jig rten kun na shes la mkhas rab mi 'jigs pa// 'jig rten 'du shes gnas la 'jug par mi byed de// de dag chos
30a7(phal chen): kun 'di la 'du shes gang zhes rtog/ de ltar gzhigs na dus gsum gang yang dmigs pa med// sngon gyi mthar thug 'das pa'i dus la rab zhugs te// phyi ma'i mthar thug ma 'ongs pa la rab
30b1(phal chen): zhugs nas/ / zhing rnams kun na ci yod kun kyang de bzhin du// shin tu shes kyang rtag par gang yang mi dmigs so// mya ngan 'das pa'i dbyings la'ang brtson par de bzhin gnas// nyon mongs med
30b2(phal chen): pa'i tshul gyi rjes song mi gnas te/ / de dag yang dag mtha' 'dra de la 'dra ba med// byang chub sprod pa las kyang dpa' bo mi ldog go// gang rnams byang chub brtan pa'i ri rab bzhin gnas shing //
30b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas rgyal sras mkhas pas chos dbyings thams cad dang // 'gro ba kun tu shin tu gang byas pa// 'di ni dpa' bo rnams kyi spyod pa'i mchog yon no// blo mchog dam pa gang zhig thams cad
30b4(phal chen): mkhyen pa yi/ / rnam grol mdzes pa'i tshul mchog yangs pa 'dod pa ni// des ni gang las zag zad srid gsum bde 'byung ba'i// byang chub sems la rim pa med par 'jug par gyis// gang gi
30b5(phal chen): bsam pa rdul bral byang chub sems gnas pa/ / de dag yon tan legs pa zad par brjod mi nus// 'on kyang 'gro ba'i don du bde gshegs legs brjod phyir// yon tan ldan pa de yi spong ba'i
30b6(phal chen): mchog kyang nyon/ / gang gis zhing rnams bye ba khrag khrig rdul byas te// phyogs rnams re re kun tu bkang ste bgrang byas shing // de yi rjes su dpag pas rnam 'dren zad byed na// 'du shes rnams
30b7(phal chen): ni mthar thug zad par mi 'gyur ro/ / gang zhig sems can grangs mkhas sems can 'du shes med// spyod pa tsam du gzhol zhing sgra la ma chags par// gang zhig 'jig rten khams 'byed chags
31a1(phal chen): pa med pa'i sems/ / de dag ldang dang grangs mkhas grangs dmig med pa yin// yid kyis nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' yas rgya che dang // dus rnams 'jig rten kun tu
31a2(phal chen): / rtogs pa'i mkhas pa gang // skar mos thal gtor bzhin du the tshom rnam gtor ba// de dag sangs rgyas chos rtogs yid can chags pa med// gang dag phyogs rnams mtha' yas zhing la rab
31a3(phal chen): 'jug cing / / sems bskyed gcig gis blo nyams med par 'dod byed pa// de dag tha dang grangs la rtogs pas der zhugs te// skye ba med pa'i chos la yang dag mtha' ltar mkhas// gang
31a4(phal chen): zhigs sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig pas ma yas pa'i/ / 'khor du nye bar phyin te zham ring 'khor gnas shing // gtso bo dag la 'dra ba'i thog mar gang 'gro ba// spyod yul mchog can de yi smon
31a5(phal chen): lam mchog 'di yin/ / gang zhig phyogs rnams kun gyi mgon po kun dran zhing // chos nyid de la nam yang gnas par ma gyur pa// khams gsum dge ba gang yong kun gyi rgyu yin te// de dag
31a6(phal chen): zhing rnams thams cad yongs su dag par sbyong / / gang rnams skye ba'i rgyud du srid gsum sna tshogs rnams// 'jig rten kun na yod la ma chags mig gyur pa// de dag bag chags mkhas shing
31a7(phal chen): de bzhin dbang po mkhas/ / mos pa bye ba khrag khrig bsam yas de bzhin mkhas// 'gro ba'i bsam pa ji bzhin gang gis shes gyur cing // shes rab chen po de dag de bzhin chos ston pa//
31b1(phal chen): de dag kun nas nyon mongs rnam dag tshul la mkhas// sems can mang po rnam par sbyor ba'i lam ldan ston// gang zhig ting 'dzin bye ba khrag khrig brjod byas rnams// sems kyi rgyu ba gcig gis
31b2(phal chen): rjes su zhugs gyur pa/ / de dag mtshan ma sna tshogs gnas pa rab tu shes// ldang ba'i rgyas la mkhas shing blo gros spyod yul shes// chags med byang chub de la mngon du gang zhugs shing //
31b3(phal chen): 'gro la phan pa'i don du blo yangs su zhugs pa// ye shes 'byam klas de dang de dag ldan pa yin// de phyir de dag skye bu mchog gi gsung yang sgrog/ gang zhig bskal pa ring dang bskal pa bud
31b4(phal chen): mkhas shing / / nyin zhag mkhas shing de bzhin zla ba zla phyed mkhas// gang yang 'jig rten rtag tu skye ba mkhas gyur pa// zhing gi rnam pa mkhas shing rnam phye'i chos med pa'o// gang rnams
31b5(phal chen): phyogs la zhugs te phyogs kyi rjes 'brang zhing / / phyogs kun tshad ni rjes su shes par ma gyur pa// de dag dbu mas phyogs kyi rjes su 'gro byed cing // zhing rnams sbyong yang yongs su ngag rdog
31b6(phal chen): chags pa med/ / stobs la 'jug pas rgyal ba rnams kyi stobs shes pas// 'gro ba rnams kyi gnas dang gnas min bsam byas na// 'das dang ma 'ongs da ltar byung ba'i las kyis/
31b7(phal chen): yang dag rtogs byas las kyi rnam par smin la gnas// 'jig rten kun khams sna tshogs tha dad ji bzhin du// sing gsum rnam par rgyu ba'i tshul yang ji bzhin dang // dbang po rnon po 'bring
32a1(phal chen): dang dbang po tha mar yang / / 'gro ba ma lus kun gyi dbang po rnam par 'byed// mos pa rnam pa sna tshogs dge dang mi dge dang // bzang ngan de bzhin 'bring la rnam par
32a2(phal chen): sems byed cing / / 'gro ba'i kun tu 'gro ba brtan pa rnam par 'byed// srid gsum rgyu yi rgyud kyang de dag rab tu shes// bsam gtan rnam par nyon mongs ji bzhin mtshan ma mthong //
32a3(phal chen): nyon mongs mtshams sbyor rnam byang cis 'gyur dang // sngan chad gnas kyi bde dang sdug bsngal rgyud rnams kyang // brtan pa rnams ni sangs rgyas stobs rnams slong ba byed// ji ltar 'gro ba'i
32a4(phal chen): lam rgyud nyon mongs las 'jug dang / / 'gro rgyud thams cad 'jig cing zhir 'gyur thams cad dang // zag pa sna tshogs rnams kyang ji ltar skyer 'gyur pa// bag chags mtshams sbyor
32a5(phal chen): ji bzhin de bzhin rab tu 'jug/ ji ltar 'jig rten nyon mongs zad cing dag 'gyur ba// de la skyes bu khyu mchog spyod pa'i blo dang ldan// stobs 'chang dag ni stobs bcu rnams kyi 'od snang
32a6(phal chen): ste/ / rgyal ba'i stobs kyang thob min the tshom yod pa min// spu rtse gcig la gang rnams rnam par sems byed cing // la la nyon mongs la la dag dang yangs pa yi// sna tshogs
32a7(phal chen): zhing rnams tshad las 'das pa kun mthong nas/ / las dang bya ba sna tshogs rgyud du rab tu shes// gang rnams rdul gcig rtse la rnam sems brjod med pa'i// zhing dang bde gshes
32b1(phal chen): sras rnams sems can gtso mthong yang / / zhing rnams 'khrugs shing 'dres pa'i nyes pa gang yang med// gcig la 'jug pas rnal 'byor ldan pa kun la 'jug/ spu gcig rtse la phyogs
32b2(phal chen): bcu thams cad rnam phye ste/ / nam mkha'i dbyings thug 'jig rten khams rnams kun zhugs shing // phyogs 'ga' tsam yang rgyal bas stong par mthong ba med// de bzhin zhing dang 'jig
32b3(phal chen): rten 'byam klas de dag sbyong / / / shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo bam po nyi shu bzhi pa// / de ltar brtan pas rgyal bas stong min zhing shes nas//
32b4(phal chen): 'jig rten kun kyang spu rtse gcig la yod par 'jug/ dus gsum rgyud rnams mtshan nyid za dang khams kun dang // nyin zhag dus dang bla phyed rgyud kyi rnam par 'jug/ de ltar rgyal zas 'jig
32b5(phal chen): med byang chub sems dpa'i rnams/ / skyes bu khyu mchog ye shes rgyal srid thob zhugs pa// de dag 'di 'dra shes nas rjes su sems byed cing // bde gshegs rnams la dga' ba
32b6(phal chen): mtha' las yangs pa 'thob/ / gang rnams bye ba khrag khrig sna tshogs lus bsgyur cing // phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba thams cad mngon par mchod pa'i phyir// rnam 'phrul dam pa bzang po
32b7(phal chen): kun tu ston byed pa/ / de dag mgon po rnams kyi spyod yul rab la zhugs// gang rnams sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig drung bslabs shing // gang rnams chos kyi mdzod rtogs yid la ngoms
33a1(phal chen): med de/ / gang dag mgon po khyu mchog rnams la dga' sems pa// de dag chos kyi sprin yin spyod pa mang la spyod// ye shes 'phel bar 'gyur ba'i chos kyi gnas
33a2(phal chen): mkhas pa/ / de dag sangs rgyas 'byung gnas ting 'dzin thob pa yin// ri rgyal lta bu de dag dad pa'i 'byung gnas rten// ye shes 'byung gnas 'gro ba'i yon tan 'byung gnas so// gnas pa
33a3(phal chen): med pa dam pa shin tu yangs pa dang / / thams cad mkhyen la mngon gyur mya ngan med pa dang // sems can skyob cing nyon mongs rnyog pa med zhugs pa'i// byams pa'i bsam pas 'gro ba kun kyang
33a4(phal chen): 'gengs/ / de dag snying rje'i blo yang shin tu yangs pa yin// bdag la cir sems de bzhin sangs rgyas sems can la// gzhan du nam mkha' lta bur mtshan nyid med par 'jug/ nyams par
33a5(phal chen): gyur pa'i sems can rnams mthong phyir zhing rtsom/ / byang chub sems la mkhas pa dag gi tshad dag ni// bskal pa bye ba'i mthas kyang brjod par mi nus te// ci phyir zhe na de las sangs rgyas thams
33a6(phal chen): cad byung / / dbang bdes rim gror byas dang rang rgyal kun kyang byung // phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams grangs med bcur ni bgrangs gyur pa'i// sems can thams cad bskal pa gcig tu bder bkod
33a7(phal chen): cing / / bslab pa bcu dang dge bcu bsam gtan 'thob pa dang // tshangs pa dag dang rnam grol zhi ba'i gnas bkod cing // de dag bskal pa bye bar bde bar rab bkod de// dgra bcom nyon mongs
33b1(phal chen): zhi la rab tu dgod byas kyang / / byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i tshogs kyi char mi rung // byang chub sems dpa' zhugs ma thag tu tshogs chen sogs// nyon mongs med cing shin tu phra lam rtogs
33b2(phal chen): pa yi/ / rang rgyal sems can bye ba khrag khrig bkod gyur kyang // bsod nams bsags pa des ni byang chub sems rab la// grangs dang cha dang bgrang ba'i rnam par nyer mi 'gro// zhing gi rdul
33b3(phal chen): ni tshad kyis shes par rung yang srid/ / skad cig sems kyis zhing mang yongs su 'das byas shing // de ltar bskal pa brjod byas zad par 'gro byas na// zhing mtha' thug par rung ming byang chub sem
33b4(phal chen): mchog min/ / mtha' rnams kun tu bskal pa mang po'i mtha' med de// sngon gyi mthar gyur paskal pa de bzhin ma 'ongs dang // da ltar byung ba'i bskal pa zad dang thug med pa'i// bskal pa
33b5(phal chen): de dag zang srid byang chub sems ma yin/ / ci phyir zhe na 'di ltar phyogs rnams kun bkang zhing // rtog dang rnam rtog yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir// skad cig gcig gis dus gsum rtogs
33b6(phal chen): par bya don du/ / 'gro ba'i don du 'dod cing sems mchog rin chen skye// phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams stong mang kun tu mtha' yas pa'o// 'gro ba rnams kyi mos pa bsam pa ci 'dra dang //
33b7(phal chen): sbyor ba gang dang sems dang spyod pa de bzhin te// mthar thug rung sring mkha' 'dra'i byang chub sems mtha' min// de ni 'di ltar phyogs bcu byams dang snying rje dang // bsam pa chen pos 'gro ba
34a1(phal chen): thams cad rgyas byas shing / / thar pa'i don du sangs rgyas yon tan kun sbyar phyir// rin chen sems kyi stobs ni tshad med rab tu skyes// mos dang bsam pa yid bzhin yang
34a2(phal chen): dag sbyor ba dang / / 'gro ba'i dbang po sbyor ba sems dang spyod pa'i rnams// skad cig gcig gis ji bzhin rtogs par bya ba'i phyir// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes lta bu'i sems skyes
34a3(phal chen): so/ / 'gro ba'i las dang nyon mongs sna tshogs 'byam klas pa// gang gis khams gsum 'di dag tu ni skyer 'gyur ba// de dag mtha' ni phyogs bcur rnyed par rung srid kyi// byang chub sems
34a4(phal chen): kyi mchog la kun tu mtha' med do/ / ci'i phyir zhe na 'di ltar nyon mongs las bral ba'i// sems ni de bzhin gshegs pa mchod pa'i don du skye// nyon mongs grol byed de bzhin las kyi rgyud kyang
34a5(phal chen): gcod/ / dus gsum mun pa sel cing mi zed snying rjes byung // phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas mtha' yas ma lus thams cad dang // sems can mang po thams cad sems gcig bskyed pa yis
34a6(phal chen): spos dang me tog 'phreng ba byug pa dam pa dang / / gdugs dang rgyal mtshan bza' btung na bzas mchod par byed// gzhan yang gdan gyi rnam pa 'chags dam pa dang // pho brang mang po sna tshogs
34a7(phal chen): tsan dan mchog bsangs pa/ / nor bu rin chen rnam par snang bas brgyan pa dang // yid bzhin nor bu ying 'ong brgyan pas mchod byas te// de ltar bde gshegs sems can mngon par mchod byed
34b1(phal chen): pas/ / bskal pa khrag khrig brjod du med pa zad byas kyang // byang chub sems dpa'i bde bsags mthar phyin bde ba nyid// gang bsgrubs byang chub sems la mnyam par nyer mi 'gro// ji snyed
34b2(phal chen): dper brjod byas pa 'di dag thams cad kyang / / yang dag skyes pa'i byang chub sems kyi char mi rung // de yang 'di ltar dus gsum bzhugs pa'o skyes bu'i mchog/ thams cad byang chub sems
34b3(phal chen): mchog de las byung ba yin/ / byang chub sems ni chags pa med pa'i mthar phyin te// thams cad tshad la gnas kyang de la tshad yod min// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes gzhol zhing tshad med
34b4(phal chen): stobs/ / sems can rang bzhin de bzhin byang chub mthar yang phyin// byang chub sems 'di nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa ste// chos rnams kun la khyab pa chos dbyings ji bzhin no// tshad med de bzhin
34b5(phal chen): nyid kun de yi spyod yul gyur/ / des ni kun tu khyab pa sems can gtso bzhin no// de ni 'byam klas chos rnams kun la rjes su zhugs// des ni zhing rnams ma lus 'byam klas kun tu khyab// des ni shes pa
34b6(phal chen): 'byam klas thams cad rtogs par chud/ / de ni sangs rgyas 'byam klas kun dang 'gal med thob// rtag tu bsod nams bla na med pa dag dang ldan// de bzhin rtag tu tshul khrims rnam dag mi gnas ldan// rtag tu
34b7(phal chen): kun gtong rtag par rab tu dge ba ste/ / ldog pa med pa'i brtson 'grus mchog dang rab tu ldan// bsam gtan mdzod la rtag par bsam gtan 'jug pa byed// shes rab shin tu yangs pa dang yang rtag tu ldan// rgyal sras
35a1(phal chen): rnams kyis rab dam pa gang yod pa/ / de dag don du ye shes kun tu babang po byung // 'gro ba kun na skyes bu'i seng ge gang bzhugs pa// de dag gis ni byang chub sems rab byin gyis brlabs//
35a2(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin dang gzungs kyi dam pas rab tu brgyan// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam 'phrul rdzu 'phrul rnam pas brgyan// 'jog rten kun dang 'gro ba rnams kyi ji tsam tshad// nam mkha'i tshad kyang phyogs bcu dag
35a3(phal chen): tu ji tsam pa/ / de dag pas kyang byang chub sems 'di tshad med de// de las skyes bu'i seng ge kun kyang skyes shing byung // byang chub sems 'di stobs bcu rnams kyi rtsa ba ste// brtan pa bzhin yi gnas
35a4(phal chen): yin so sor shes pa'i rtsa/ / rgyal ba'i chos rnams bco brgyad yang dag 'byin pa ste// skyes bu'i gtso bos mkhyen par bya ba'i chos kun 'byin// gzugs kyi sku ni mtshan rab rnams kyis
35a5(phal chen): bsags pa dang / / chos sku mnyam nyid rtog pa mi mnga' brnyes pa dang // 'gro bas mchod pa'i ye shes chags med gang byung ba// kun gyi rtsa ba 'byung gnas byang chub sems 'di yin//
35a6(phal chen): rang rgyal theg pa 'byung zhing nyan thos theg pa'ang 'byung // bsam gtan ting 'dzin bde ba gzugs kyi khams rnams dang // gzugs med khams rnams ting nge 'dzin gyi bde ba dag/ kun
35a7(phal chen): gyi rtsa ba 'byung gnas byang chub sems mchog 'di yin no/ / mi dang de bzhin lha yi dbang po'i bde ba dang // lam rgyud sna tshogs kun kyang 'di la shin tu sbyangs// brtson 'grus stobs dang
35b1(phal chen): dbang po'i bde ba gang yod pa/ / kun gyi rtsa ba dang po byang chub sems 'di yin// ci phyir zhe na 'di ltar byang chub sems bskyed cing // pha rol phyin drug brtson par spyad pa rab tu spyod//
35b2(phal chen): sems can rnamal yang spyod pa yang dag rab tu ston// des ni khams gsum 'gro ba'i bde ba kun kyang 'byung // sangs rgyas chags med thugs chud don dam mkhyen pa'i rnams// chos
35b3(phal chen): kyi dam pa mchog rnams yang dag kun ston cing / / rgya chen nyon mongs las las sems can dgrol mdzad de// mya ngan 'das pa dam pa mchog la dgod mdzad pa// ye shes 'od zer 'ong
35b4(phal chen): yangs nyi ma lta bu ste/ / 'gro bar spyod pa dkar pos yongs rgyas zla ba bzhin// yon tan shin tu bsags pa tshad med chu zla lta bu ste// dri med chags pa mi mnga' tshad med mkha' dbyings
35b5(phal chen): 'dra/ / gang zhig yon tan mtha' yas byang chub sems yangs pa// shin tu che zhing bde skyid tshad med smin byed cing // phyi mtha'i mur thug spyod par mos pas su brtson pa// de dag
35b6(phal chen): sems can 'dul ba'i don phyir rtag tu brtson/ / 'jig rten 'byam klas thams cad rnam par sbyang ba'i phyir// smon lam bye ba khrag khrig bsam gyis mi khyab dang // stong pa mtshan ma med pa
35b7(phal chen): smon med mi gnas pa'i/ / smon lam bye ba brgyas ni sems de dag par 'gyur// chos kyi rang bzhin nam mkha' lta bu sus rtogs shing // zhi dang rab zhi nyer zhir thams cad mnyam gzhog pa// /
36a1(phal chen): de dag chos grangs khrag khrig bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i// grangs su 'gro la ston kyang de ni gnas pa med// phyogs bcu kun gyi 'jig rten gtso bo ji snyed pa// de dag kun
36a2(phal chen): gyis byang chub sems mchog 'di bsngags te/ / yon tan brgya phrag bsam gyis mi khyab pas kyang brgyan// sems can gtso bzhin yongs dag pha rol phyin pa yin// bskal pa sems can
36a3(phal chen): snyed du gal te legs brjod kyang / / byang chub sems rab de la mthar thug gang yang med// rgyal ba 'byung ba'i rigs chen der ni gang skyes pa// de yid pa ni khams gsum glongs kyang gang yang
36a4(phal chen): med/ / dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyis gang zhig rnam bsags pa'i// byang chub sems rab de la smon lam kun gyis gyis// byang chub sems rab dam pa de ni bsod nams gter// des
36a5(phal chen): ni rgyal sras chags pa med par rab tu 'thob/ / 'gro ba'i sems dang spyod pa shes shing mthong rung srid// zhing rnams rdul du rlags te bgrang bar nus kyang srid// bar snang sbra yis mnyam
36a6(phal chen): par gzhal bar nus srid kyi/ / byang chub sems mchog yon tan mthar phyin mi nus so// 'di las dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad rab tu byung // 'di las 'jig rten 'gro ba kun gyi
36a7(phal chen): bde ba 'byung / / 'di las rgyal bas bsngags pa'i legs pa thams cad 'byung // 'dis ni sems can gtso la the tshom med par 'gyur// 'dis ni 'jig rten kun gyi bsgribs pa zad par
36b1(phal chen): 'gyur/ / 'dis ni zhing rnams yongs su dag pa'i mchog tu 'gyur// 'di las 'jig rten dam pa shes dang ldan pa 'byung // gang zhig phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba blta bar 'dod pa dang //
36b2(phal chen): gang zhig byin dang bsod nams mi zad mdzod 'dod dang // gang zhig 'gro ba kun gyi sdug bsngal zlog 'dod pa// des ni yon tan mtha' yas byang chub sems bskyed bya// shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i
36b3(phal chen): mdo sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ / byang chub sems dpa' sems dang po bskyed pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po'i dpe yang dag par bsags pa tshogs su bcad pa'i le'u zhes bya ba ste nyi shu
36b4(phal chen): gnyis pa'o/ / // de nas byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus blo gros kyis// byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras
36b5(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems bskyed pa rab tu thob pa/ sems dang po bskyed pa la gnas pa/ de ltar tshad med pa'i bsod nams kyi tshogs dang ldan pa/ thams cad
36b6(phal chen): mkhyen pa'i ye shes rgya chen po la yang dag par 'dzeg pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med par shin tu chud pa/ 'jig rten kun tu khrid par byed pa// rnam par bzlog pa/ rdzogs pa'i sangs
36b7(phal chen): rgyas kyi 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos nyid kyi rjes su song ba/ 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa/ byang chub sems
37a1(phal chen): dpa'i rnam par dgod pa la shin tu nges pa/ rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rab tu gzhol ba de dag gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la ji ltar brtson par byas pa'i rnam pa gang
37a2(phal chen): gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par 'gyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par dgod pa las 'das par 'gyur ba dang // spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor chen po yongs su dag
37a3(phal chen): par 'gyur ba dang / smon lam chen po yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i gter chen po rab tu thob par 'gyur ba dang / sems can rnams la snod ji bzhin du sbyin par byed par
37a4(phal chen): 'gyur ba dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i phyogs yongasu mi gtong bar 'gyur ba dang / ji ltar dam bcas pa'i sems can rnams sgrol bar 'gyur ba dang / sangs rgyas dang / chos dang / dge 'dun gyi gdung
37a5(phal chen): mi 'chad par 'gyur ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba dmigs pa thams cad du sbyor ba don med pa mi 'gyur ba dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis de la brtson par byas nas/ chos kyi
37a6(phal chen): yul 'di dag yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur bar ji ltar brtsam par bya ba de legs par bshad pa mdzod cig/ 'khor 'di dag thams cad ni nyan par 'dod do// sems can chen po de dag gi brtson pa'i
37a7(phal chen): rnam pa ji lta bus/ ma rig pa'i mun nag thams cad bsal te/ bdud kyi dkrugs ma'i 'khor thams cad las shin tu rgyal bar byas nas/ phas kyi rgol ba thams cad zil gyis mnan te
37b1(phal chen): sems kyi dri ma kun nas nyon mongs pa'i phyogs thams cad kun nas bsal nas/ dge ba'i rtsa ba phun sum tshogs pa thams cad shin tu bsgrubs te/ mi khom pa dang / ngan song dang / ngan 'gror
37b2(phal chen): lam thams cad rnam par bzlog nas/ ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor chen po rnam par byang bar byas te/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa dang / gzungs dang / ting nge 'dzin dang /
37b3(phal chen): mngon par shes pa dang / rig pa dang / mi 'jigs pa yongs su dag pa rnams mngon par bsgrubs nas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rnam par dag pa dang / mtshan dang / dpe byang
37b4(phal chen): byad bzang po dang / sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi rgyan mngon par bsgrub pa yongs su rgyas par byas te/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi stobs dang / mi 'jigs pa dang /
37b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul rtogs par 'gyur ba dang / de ltar mngon par byang chub nas kyang / bsam pa'i
37b6(phal chen): tshul bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su grub par gyur pa dag tu/ ji ltar yongs su smin par bya ba'i sems can dag la/ dus dang dbang po'i rgyud ji lta ba bzhin du/ sangs rgyas kyi
37b7(phal chen): mdzad pa mtha' yas pa 'byin par 'gyur ba de legs par shod cig/ 'khor 'di dag thams cad ni nyan par 'dod do// ji ltar yang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis byang chub sems
38a1(phal chen): dpa'i yon tan 'di dang / gzhan dag dang / byang chub sems dpa'i chos dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam gyi yul rnams
38a2(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs par byas te/ myur du de bzhin gsheg pa'i mnyam pa nyid 'thob pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis/ bskal pa
38a3(phal chen): brgya stong grangs med par yang dag par bsgrubs pa'i chos kyi mdzod 'di yang yang dag par srung zhing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la gnas shing ston pa dang 'chad pa'i tshe/ bdud dam bdud
38a4(phal chen): kyi ris su gtogs pa dang / phas kyi rgol ba thams cad kyis zil gyis mi non pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du yang skyo ba med par dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin par byed pa dang /

38a6(phal chen): gyi dbang po dang / nam mkha' lding gi dbang po dang / mi 'am ci'i dbang po dang / lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po dang / mi'i dbang po dang / tshangs pa'i dbang pos rim gror bya ba rab tu 'thob
38a7(phal chen): pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi dbang pos rim gror bya ba rab tu 'thob pa dang / de ltar rim gror byas nas kyang 'jig rten thams cad kyis phyag bya ba/ 'jig rten thams cad kyis
38b1(phal chen): mngon par mchod pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyis dbang skur ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis shin tu dgongs pa/ byang chub sems dpa' tshogs kyis shin tu bsrung ba//
38b2(phal chen): rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba dang smon lam rab tu thob pa/ chos dkar po chen po yang dag par spel pa'i rnams/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams
38b3(phal chen): kyi chos kyi mdzod rnam par 'byed par 'gyur ba dang / dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pa rgya chen po rab tu 'byed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rim gyis spyod pa yongs su bsgrub pa shin tu ston/
38b4(phal chen): par 'gyur ba de lta bu'i gnas dag yang dag par bstan pa mdzod cig/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus blo gros kyis don 'di nyid brnan te brjod pa'i phyir/ byang chub
38b5(phal chen): sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la tshags su bcad de smras pa/ spyod la 'jug pa mtha' yas langs pa dag/ rang byung ye shes sgrub pa dge ba'i rnams// rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems
38b6(phal chen): dpa' yon tan can/ / grags pa chen po rnams la legs par shod// byang chub sems dpa' gang rnams sems thob cing // bsod nams ldan pa'i ye shes thob pa rnams//
38b7(phal chen): skyon med zhugs pa 'jig rten rnam bzlog cing // yang dag sangs rgyas chos mnyam nyid thob rnams// de dag gis ni bde gshegs bstan pa la// brtson 'grus brtan pas ji ltar brtsen
39a1(phal chen): par bya/ / gang gis phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba mnyes bya zhing // yang dag sangs rgyas sa yang gnan bya dang // spyod pa dag dang smon lam yongs dag dang // ye shes
39a2(phal chen): gter chen rab tu 'thob 'gyur zhing / / thob nas de dag 'gro kun mi gnas pas// yongs su blangs pa rtag tu gtong byed dang // gang yang pha rol phyin pa mchog gi lam// de dag mi gtong
39a3(phal chen): rab tu spyod pa dang / / sems can ji ltar sgrol byed dam bcas shing // yang dag sangs rgyas bsam pa mnyam 'dzin dang // mig gi dmigs pa brtan pa thams cad kyi// 'byung ba ston
39a4(phal chen): can la stobs 'gyur zhing / / skyes bu khyu mchog de dag brtson 'gyur ba'i// rnam dag lam de khyu mchog khyod kyis ston// ji ltar de dag mun pa kun bsal cing // 'khrug pa'i 'khor

39a6(phal chen): shes chen po'i dkyil 'khor mchog sbyong dang / / yon tan bzang po thams cad ldan gyur cing // rgyal ba'i ye shes stobs kyang 'thob 'gyur dang // skyes bu khyu mchog ye shes zhugs nas kyang /
39a7(phal chen): sems can bsam pa ji bzhin ston byed cing // mtha' yas yangs pa'i zhing rnams bsam yas su// ston pa chen po'i las kyang byed pa dang // ci nas de dag spyod pa mchog thob nas//
39b1(phal chen): mi yi khyu mchog mdzod rnams ston byed de// zil gyis mnon gzhan gyis mi 'pham par// rgyal ba'i chos nyid rtag tu 'dzin byed ston// seng ge bzhin du ji ltar 'jigs pa med// ji ltar
39b2(phal chen): zla bzhin dag pa'i mdog tu spyod/ / tshu la pad+mo bzhin du chags med pa// de dag rgyal ba'i yon tan ji ltar skyong // de skad ces smras pa dang // byang chub sems dpa' chos
39b3(phal chen): kyi blo gros kyis byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus blo gros la 'di skad ces smras so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras khyod ni skye bo mang po la phan pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / 'jig rten
39b4(phal chen): la snying brtse ba dang / lha dang mi rnams kyi don dang / phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir zhugs pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar khyod byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa shin tu rtogs shing / rnam par

39b6(phal chen): ldog pa med pas shin tu byung ba 'dri bar byed pa ni/ kye rgyal ba'i sras legs so legs so// kye rgyal ba'i sras de'i phyir shin tu legs par nyon la yid la zung zhig dang / sangs rgyas

40a1(phal chen): kyis/ sog mar sems bskyed pa de mi nyams par yongs su bsrung ba dang / rim gror bya ba'i phyir bag yod par bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras de la rnam pa bcus ni/ byang
40a2(phal chen): chub sems dpa' bag yod pa la gnas pa zhes bya ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ tshul khrims kyi phung po shin tu bsrungs pa dang / byang chub kyi sems ma nyams shing shin tu sbyangs pa dang / byang chub
40a3(phal chen): sems dpa'i bsam pa g.yo dang sgyu med par blta ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba sbyor ba phyir mi ldog pa dang / rang gi sems bskyed pa shin tu rtogs pa dang / phyogs khyim pa dang / so so'i skye bo dang
40a4(phal chen): ma 'dres pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba las 'jig rten gyi 'du shes dang / 'dod pa thams cad dang bral ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa spangs pa rab

40b2(phal chen): ji ltar thos pa'i chos la tshul bzhin du rtog par zhugs pa yin/ bsam gtan gyi rjes su song ba'i sems kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo'i rjes su song ba yin/

42a1(phal chen): rnam par dgod pa thams cad la mkhas pa rnam par spyod pa yin/ chos kyi sgo gang gis gang khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / ye shes kyi sgo gang gis thob par 'gyur ba dang / bsgrub
