93b4(phal chen): mthas gtugs par lus byin gyis brlab pa/ 'gro ba thams cad du khyab pa/ tshad med pa mi gnas pa'ang rab tu shes te/ bdag gi lus de dag la'ang zhing thams cad
93b5(phal chen): yongs su 'dus par kun tu ston cing / dus gsum gyi sems can thams cad dang / chos thams cad dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyang rab tu ston to// sems can de dag gi
93b6(phal chen): 'du shes kyi rgyud dang mthu la'ang rab tu 'jug go/ / sems can de dag gi bsam pa dang / mos pa dang / las dang / rnam par smin pa rnam par dag pa ji tsam pa de tsam du/ sems
93b7(phal chen): can gdul ba'i don du lus byin gyis rlob ste/ de yang 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i ni sgyu ma lta bu'i chos thams cad kyis shin tu sprul pa ste/ mig yor lta bu'i sangs rgyas skye
94a1(phal chen): bar bya ba la pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ / 'gro ba thams cad mi lam lta bur rtogs pa'i yid dang ldan pa'o// don dang yi ge'i tshogs pa mi zad pa'i mdzod do//
94a2(phal chen): dran pas dbang sgyur ba'i chos thams cad la nges par rtogs thob pa'o// shes rab che ba'i ting nge 'dzin thams cad la yang rab tu zhugs pa'o// gnyis su med pa'i sa la rgyud
94a3(phal chen): kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pa'o/ / sems can gyi khams gnyis la gnas pa la snying rje chen por gnas pa ste/ chos de lta bu dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i ni stobs bcu
94a4(phal chen): mthar dben par gyur pa ste/ chos kyi byings mig 'dru la lta bu la rab tu 'jug cing gnas pa'o// chags pa med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa yongs su rdzogs pa'o//

94a7(phal chen): rab tu zhugs pa'o/ / 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo'i byin gyis brlabs dang ldan pa'o// sangs rgyas thams
94b1(phal chen): cad kyi chos rgya mtsho'i tshul gyi rjes pa zhugs shing gting rnyed pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'don byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bcu /

95a4(phal chen): chos 'di nyid bstan par snang ngo / / phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa'i pha rol nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas

95a6(phal chen): nyid 'di ston pa legs so legs so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bdag cag kun kyang ming yon tan dang ldan pa zhes bya ba dag ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan kun tu yon tan zhes bya

99a4(phal chen): chos rnams thams cad zhi la bzod pa yin/ / mi sgul sems dang mnyam pa'i rnams// mtha' yas shes can de dag spyod 'di'o// 'jig rten khams ni gcig nas kyang // de dag lus ni g.yo zhing
99a5(phal chen): 'pho bar mi byed par/ / 'gro ba kun tu 'ang snang ba'i rnams// mtha' yas lus can de dag spyod 'di yin// gang zhig zhing gi tshul rnams kun// rjes su 'jug pa shin tu phra bar rab shes kyang //
99a6(phal chen): yongs su rgyas bya'i blo med pa// mtha' yas sems pa de dag spyod 'di'o// gnas dang gnas min shes gyur cing // stobs la 'jug pa dag tu shin tu zhugs pa rnams// stobs kyi dam pa 'dzin pa
99a7(phal chen): dag/ stobs kyis stobs che de dag spyod 'di'o// 'das pa dag dang ma 'ongs dang // da ltar byang ba'i las rnams shin tu 'byams klas la// rtag tu shes pa 'jug gyur pa// tshul shes de dag spyod pa
99b1(phal chen): 'di yin no/ / 'gro ba'i dus dang dus min pa// ji ltar sems can 'dul bar 'gyur ba de bzhin shes// dus la 'bebs par mkhas pa'i rnams// shes pa de dag spyod pa 'di yin no//
99b2(phal chen): chos la spyod pa kun srung zhing // lus dang ngag yid kyi rnams kyang srung byed pa// bdud kyi lam du ma zhugs pa// shes pa'i blo can de dag spyod 'di'o// rnam par gzhag pa'i rgyus mkhas pa//
99b3(phal chen): chos rnams la ni ji ltar spobs par 'jug pa rnams// de bzhin nyid dang yul mnyam pa// bde gshegs spyod pa de dag spyod 'di yin// chags med mdzod la brtson pa dag/ gzungs kyi sgo mo'i
99b4(phal chen): dkyil 'khor rab tu shes pa'i rnams/ / chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa yi// rjes su zhugs pa de dag spong 'di yin// dus gsum gshegs pa'i rgyal ba rnams// ji snyed bzhugs pa kun dang gcig/
99b5(phal chen): sems yid ldan pa// rang bzhin gcig tu rtogs pa'i rnams// chags med rigs can de dag spyod 'di'o// bsgribs med ye shes tshul shes shing // bsgribs med ye shes phyag rgya dag la zhugs
99b6(phal chen): pa'i rnams/ / bsgribs med mig kyang bdog byed pa// mig can de dag spyod pa 'di yin no// gnyis su med la spyod pa yi// rdzu 'phrul rnam par gzhog pa'i mgon po thams cad kun// rnam par 'phrul
99b7(phal chen): pa mkhyen pa'i rnams/ / gnyis su med spyod de dag spyod 'di'o// chos kyi sprin ni mtha' yas pa'i// char chen rab tu 'bebs shing zhing rnams yangs par rgyu// don rnams thams cad rtogs gyur pa/
100a1(phal chen): chos sprin de dag spyod yul 'di yin no// dad pa phyir ldog mi 'gyur zhing // rtsa ba shin tu tshugs shing dad pa nas dag pa// rnam par shes pa thams cad la// bslabs pa
100a2(phal chen): rnams kyi spyod yin mnyan par gyis/ / 'gro ba 'di dag ji snyed pa// ma lus thams cad sems bskyed gcig tu chud byas te// sems kyi rang bzhin shes pa'i rnams// rang bzhin med pa de dag spyod 'dra
100a3(phal chen): yin/ / zhing rnams bsam gyis mi khyab pa// chos kyi dbyings rnams kun tu gang gis sprul byas shing // mnyan pa med par der spyod pa// dpe med 'gro ldan de dag spyod 'di'o// sangs rgyas zhing
100a4(phal chen): rnams mtha' yas te/ / de dag kun na 'jig rten mgon po gang bzhugs pa// de rnams dang ni mngon sum du// sangs rgyas zhabs kyi drung na 'khod 'gyur pa// de dag lus ni gcig pur yang // ting nge
100a5(phal chen): 'dzin la mnyam par gzhag pa rab tu ston/ / lus ni stong phrag mtha' yas pa// ting nge 'dzin las ldang na shin tu snang // spyod pa zab dang ldan byas nas// spros pa med pa'i spyod pa dag la rab spyod pa
100a6(phal chen): dga' ba'i yid dang ldan pa'i rnams/ / sems can kun la dga' bar byed pa yin// dbang po tha dad tshul rnams la// blo gros gnas shing shes pa rab tu thob pa'i rnams// dbang po dag ni mi gnas
100a7(phal chen): pa/ / ma dus dul ba 'di dag spyod 'di yin// tha dad chos kyi tshul rnams la// chos rnams thams cad kun la dbang bas shes gyur pa// kun kyang sangs rgyas mdzad pa la// dmigs pa'i cho gas
100b1(phal chen): rab tu spyod pa yin/ / shin tu yangs pa'i ljags mnga' ba// de dag dbang po rnams dang legs pa'i spyod thob na// su yi sems shig dang mi 'gyur// nam mkha' lta bu de dag spyod 'di yin//
100b2(phal chen): tu mtha' yas shes ldan zhing // chos rnams kun la kun tu mtha' las mig yod pa// ye shes mtha' yas tshul ldan pa// mtha' yas shes can de dag spyod 'di yin// zad mi nus pa zang byed ci
100b3(phal chen): bsod nams 'byam klas yod pas bsod nams mi zad pa/ / 'gro ba dag pa'i mthar phyin rnams// 'dra med de dag spyod pa 'di yin no// tshogs dang ldan zhing 'jig rten dang // de dag chos kyi lam la
100b4(phal chen): rab tu 'jug byas kyang / / de dag sems can 'du shes med// sems can bye ba khrag khrig rab tu 'grel// nyon mongs med pa rtogs shes shing // spyod pa mngon par shes pa thams cad mthong ba'i
100b5(phal chen): rnams/ / bde ba'i lam rnams ston byed pa// mig can de dag tshul ni 'di yin no// sangs rgyas ye shes spyod pa dang // tshad med yon tan dam pa thob par gyur pa'i rnams// mi 'jigs pa ni rnyed
100b6(phal chen): gyur pa/ / shes can de dag tshul ni 'di yin no// 'jug pa kun la rab zhugs shing // zhing la 'jug dang chos kyi dbang la zhugs gyur pa// sems can zhugs la gnas byas nas// sems
100b7(phal chen): can dam pa sems can 'grol bar byed/ / phyogs rnams kun tu chos kyi rnga// brdungs shing 'jig rten 'di dag ston byed pa'i// chos rab sbyin pa'i bdag po rnams// nyams me togs byed
101a1(phal chen): de dag spyod 'di yin/ / skyil mo kyang 'dug gcig gis kyang // zhing yangs brjod du med pa kun ka rgyas byed kyang // su yi lus la gnod byed pa// chos sku ldan pa de dag sgo
101a2(phal chen): 'di yin/ / don dang yi ge gcig la yang // shin tu bstan pa bye ba khrag khrig rjes su 'brang // de dag mtha' ni rnyed mi nus// mnyam med shes ldan de dag spyod 'di yin// bsgribs pa med pa'i
101a3(phal chen): tshul shes pa/ / sangs rgyas rnam thar tshul la shin tu bslabs pa'i rnams// 'jigs pa med par gyur pa dag/ tshad med de dag tshul ni 'di yin no// de dag phyogs rnams rgya mtsho dang // zhing
101a4(phal chen): rnams rgya mtsho mtha' ma dag dang dbus med par/ / shes pa rgya mtsho ldan pa yi// chos rnams rgya mtshos 'jig rten tshim par byed// gang rnams gshegs shing skyer 'gyur dang // byang chub rnam par
101a5(phal chen): 'tshang rgya 'gro ba kun dag tu/ / su zhig mngon par snang gyur pa// mtha' dbus med pa 'di dag spyod 'di yin// mya ngan 'da' ba du ma yang // zhing rnams bye ba khrag khrig dag na mngon par snang // 'on kyang smra /
101a6(phal chen): ba'i seng ge rnams// mya ngan mi 'da' smon las phyir mi ldog/ chos rnams lhun ni gcig gyur cing // sems can kun dang lus kyang gcig tu gyur pa'i rnams// rgyal ba dag la rtog med pas// lus bci/
101a7(phal chen): gyur pa spyod 'di yin// tshig dang don rnams tha dad pas// 'jig rten khams rnams mtha' dang dbus yod ma yin par// rang bzhin gcig la mos pa dag/ dus gsum shes pa de dag spyod 'di yin//
101b1(phal chen): sems can dag dang rgyal ba dang // chos kyi tshul rnams kun la zad pa med rnyed pa// sangs rgyas byin la mos pa dag/ rgyal bas byin brlabs de dag spyod 'di yin// chags pa med pa'i sku 'dra zhing // chags pa med pa'i
101b2(phal chen): mig gi pha rol phyin pa'i rnams/ / chags med rna ba mkhas pa dang // chags med yid can de dag spyod pa de yin// mngon shes thams cad rnyed pa dang // ye shes mngon par shes pa'i rjes su song ba'i rnams//
101b3(phal chen): ye shes kun gyi dpal ldan pa// shes pa bzang can de dag spyod 'di yin// shin tu mnyam gzhag sems ldan zhing // ye shes mtha' yas shes rab shin tu che ba sa rnams// kun tu spyod yul ldan pa dag
101b4(phal chen): thams cad gzigs pa de dag spyod 'di yin/ / yon tan kun gyi mthar phyin pa// sems can yangs pa gcig nas gcig brgyud sgrol ba'i rnams// yid ni yongs su nyams med pa// rtag tu brtson pa de dag
101b5(phal chen): spyod 'di yin/ / kun mkhyen thams cad gzigs pa dag/ sangs rgyas thams cad dus gsum gshegs pa mgon po yi// rigs dang brgyud du skyes pa'i rnams// rgyal sras de dag spyod pa 'di yin no//
101b6(phal chen): rjes su bstan la brtson byed pa// phas kyi rgol ba'i lam la 'jigs med spyod pa dag/ mtha' yas blo yi spyod pa dang // sangs rgyas byang chub rjes su zhugs pa'i rnams// mtha' dbus med pa'i
101b7(phal chen): zhing gi rnams/ / thams cad kun tu snang ba gcig gis gsal bar byed// thams cad snang bar byed pa'i rnams// mun pa sel ba'i spyod pa 'di yin no// gang du rgyal bas mdzad 'os pa/
102a1(phal chen): der ni sems can khrag khrig shin tu 'dul byed cing // sangs rgyas sgyu dang sangs rgyas zhing // sangs rgyas rgyan can khrag khrig snang bar byed// spyod pa dag ni mtha' yas la/
102a2(phal chen): su gnas brtan pa de dag shes pa ji ltar rung // spyod pa thams cad shin tu ston// 'gro bar spyod pa thams cad mthar thug byed// chos kyi dbyings dang mnyam pa yin// bdag gi lus ni brjod du med par
102a3(phal chen): gyur pa yis/ / de dag legs par brjod byas kyang // bskal pa khrag khrig dag gis mi zad do// yon tan kun tu mtha' yas shing // yon tan mchog rnams thams cad mtha' yas pa'i// yon te
102a4(phal chen): kun ni brjod yas te/ / thub pas bskal par gsungs kyang zad mi 'gyur// rang rgyal rnams dang nyan thos la// gzhol bar gyur pa'i 'jig rten gzhan gyi rnams kyis lta// bskal pa brjod yas brjod
102a5(phal chen): byas kyang / / zad par mi nus de ni smos ci dgos// shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las// yon tan gyi me tog shin tu bsags pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa
102a6(phal chen): bstan pa'i le'u ste nyi shu drug pa'o/ / // de nas byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pas// yang byang chub sems dpa' de dag la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag
102a7(phal chen): bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gter yin te/ / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang // ma byon pa dang // da ltar byung ba rnams kyis gsungs so// gsung ngo // gsung bar
102b1(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ / bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dad pa'i gter dang / tshul khrims kyi gter dang / ngo tsha shes pa'i gter dang / khrel yod pa'i gter dang / zos pa'i gter dang / gtong ba'i gter dang
102b2(phal chen): dam 'cha' ba'i gter dang / rtogs pa'i gter dang / blo gros kyi gter dang / blo'i gter te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i gter bcu po de dag
102b3(phal chen): ni 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs so// gsung ngo // gsung bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la dad pa'i
102b4(phal chen): gter gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad stong pa zhes bya bar dad par byed do// chos thams cad mtshan ma med pa zhes bya bar dad par byed do// chos
102b5(phal chen): thams cad smon pa med pa zhes bya bar dad par byed do/ / chos thams cad ma byas pa zhes bya bar dad par byed do// chos thams cad ma rtags pa zhes bya bar dad par byed do// chos thams cad gnas pa med
102b6(phal chen): pa zhes bya bar dad par byed do/ / chos thams cad tshad med pa zhes bya bar dad par byed do// chos thams cad bla na med pa zhes bya bar dad par byed do// chos thams cad 'dar mi rung ba zhes bya bar dad par byed
102b7(phal chen): chos thams cad 'byung ba med pa zhes bya bar dad par byed do/ / de ni chos dang 'thun pa'i dad pa dang ldan pa yin te/ chos thams cad bsam gyis mi khyab bo zhes bya bas zhum par mi 'gyur ro//
103a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad bsam gyis mi khyab po zhes bya bas zhum par mi 'gyur ro// sems can gyi khams thams cad bsam gyis mi khyab bo zhes bya bas zhum par mi 'gyur ro// chos
103a2(phal chen): kyi dbyings bsam gyis mi khyab bo zhes bya bas zhum par mi 'gyur ro/ / nam mkha' dbyings bsam gyis mi khyab bo zhes bya bas zhum par mi 'gyur ro// mya ngan las 'da' ba'i dbyings bsam gyis mi khyab bo/
103a3(phal chen): zhes bya bas zhum par mi 'gyur ro// 'das pa'i dus bsam gyis mi khyab po zhes bya bas zhum par mi 'gyur ro// ma 'ongs pa'i dus bsam gyis mi khyab po zhes bya bas zhum par mi 'gyur ro// da ltar byung
103a4(phal chen): ba'i dus bsam gyis mi khyab bo zhes bya bas zhum par mi 'gyur ro/ / bskal pa thams cad la 'jug pa bsam gyis mi khyab bo zhes bya bas zhum par mi 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de'i dad pa ni sangs
103a5(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis ji ltar mkhyen pa bzhin du gcig tu nges par gyur pa yin te/ sangs rgyas ye shes kyi mtha' yang zad mi shes so// 'jig rten gyi khams rnams kyang zad mi shes te/
103a6(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams re rer yang mtha' yas pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas so// mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// mngon par
103a7(phal chen): 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro/ / yang dag par byung ngo // yang dag par 'byung ngo // yang dag par 'byung bar 'gyur ro// yongs su mya ngan la 'das so// yongs su mya ngan las 'da' 'o// yongs su mya ngan las
103b1(phal chen): 'da' bar 'gyur te/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes de ni 'bri ba 'am/ 'phel ba 'am/ skye ba 'am/ 'gag pa 'am/ 'pho ba 'am/ 'gro ba 'am/ nye bar byed pa 'am/ ring bar byed pa 'am/ shes
103b2(phal chen): par byed pa 'am/ 'byan par byed pa ma yin te/ de ni sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la yang dag par gnas pas/ zad pa med cing mtha' yas pa'i dad pa'i gter dang ldan pa yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras
103b3(phal chen): dag/ dad pa 'di ni mtha' yas pa// kun tu mtha' yas pa/ mi zad pa/ phyir mi ldog pa myu gur gyur pa ma yin pa/ tha dad pa ma yin pa/ ma 'dres pa/ rtsa ba brtan pa/ 'phags pa dang
103b4(phal chen): 'thun pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi brgyud du gyur pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs yang dag par 'dzin pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi mos pa yang dag par bskyed pa/
103b5(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i rjes su song ba/ nges par rtogs pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs la mkhas par gyur pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di ni byang chub
103b6(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi dad pa'i gter te/ de la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad thos par gyur na bden par khong du chud de/ sems
103b7(phal chen): can thams cad la rnam par 'byed pa'i phyir nan tan byed par 'gyur ro/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi gter gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i
104a1(phal chen): sras dag/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' thog mar phun sum tshogs pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin/ byin gyis ma brlabs pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin/ mi gnas pa'i
104a2(phal chen): tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin/ lhag par lta ba med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin/ 'gal ba med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin/ gzhan la mi gnod pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin/ sa 'dres
104a3(phal chen): pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin/ nye ba'i nyon mongs pa med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin/ skyon med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin/ kha na ma tho ba med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/
104a4(phal chen): ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' thog mar phun sum tshogs pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' thog ma nyid du sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde
104a5(phal chen): bar sems so/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' byin gyis ma brlabs pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ mu stegs can gyi gnas pa dang mi 'dra ba'i tshul khrims yin te/ de ni
104a6(phal chen): 'di ltar rang bzhin gyis dus gsum mnyam pa nyid du go cha bgos shing spyod pa'o/ / ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di la 'dod pa'i khams
104a7(phal chen): la mi gnas pa'i tshul khrims can yin/ gzugs kyi khams la mi gnas pa'i tshul khrims can yin/ gzugs med pa'i khams la mi gnas pa'i tshul khrims can yin/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'khor ba de
104b1(phal chen): ngag la bdag gir bya ba med de/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mi gnas pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' lhag par lta ba med pa'i tshul khrims
104b2(phal chen): dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' 'gyod pa med pa'i rgyu dang ldan pa yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar mtshams med pa'i las mngon par 'du mi byed de/ tshul khrims lhod pa la gzhol
104b3(phal chen): ba ma yin no/ / de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' lhag par lta ba med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'gal ba med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang
104b4(phal chen): chub sems dpa' ma bcas pa ni 'cha' bar mi byed/ bcas pa ni gcod par mi byed de/ de ni mya ngan las 'das pa'i mthar thug zug tu ji ltar 'thun pa'i chos dang ldan pa yin no// gang gis pha rol gyi sdug
104b5(phal chen): bsngal gyi rgyur 'gyur pa dang / pha rol 'khrug par 'gyur ba'i tshul khrims de lta bu dam bca' ba la dam bcas shing mi gnas te/ de ni 'di ltar pha rol gyi sems dad par bya ba'i phyir tshul khrims yang
104b6(phal chen): dag par len par byed do/ / ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' gzhan la mi gnod pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems can thams cad gtse ba'i phyir tshul khrims
104b7(phal chen): kyi rig sngags dang / gsang sngags dang / sman gyi sbyor ba de lta bu mi sgrub kyi/ de ni sems can thams cad bskyab pa'i phyir tshul khrims yang dag par blangs te gnas so// ji ltar na byang
105a1(phal chen): chub sems dpa' ma 'dres pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' chad par lta ba dang / rtag par lta ba dang / 'dres pa'i tshul khrims yang dag
105a2(phal chen): par len par mi byed de/ de ni 'di ltar rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba la rten pa'i tshul khrims yang dag par len to// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin
105a3(phal chen): zhe na/ yon tan med pa bstan par bya ba'i phyir gzhan gyi sems la lta zhing rtog pa rnam pa sna tshogs su 'gyur ba ma yin no// de ni 'di ltar chos kyis ngoms pa dang ldan pa yin te/ 'byung ba'i lam tshol zhing
105a4(phal chen): sbyor ba'i tshul khrims yang dag par blangs te gnas so/ / ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' skyon med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' tshul khrims dang log pa'i tshul
105a5(phal chen): khrims nye bar bzung ste/ gang gis pha rol po dma' ba'i tshul can du gyur par bdag la mi bstod gzhan la mi smod do// de ni 'di ltar g.yeng ba med pa nye bar bzung ste/ tshul khrims yang dag par
105a6(phal chen): blangs shing gnas so/ / ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' kha na ma tho ba med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' srog gcod pa yongs su spangs pa yin te/ ma byin par
105a7(phal chen): len pa dang / 'dod pas log par g.yem pa dang / brdzun du smra ba dang / phra ma'i tshig dang / dag brlang ba dang / tshig 'khyal ba dang / chags sems dang / gnod sems dang / log par lta ba sangs
105b1(phal chen): su spangs pa yin te/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam yang dag par blangs te gnas so// de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' kha na ma tho ba med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin/ de 'di snyam du sems bskyed de/
105b2(phal chen): gang ji snyam du sems can rnams tshul khrims ngan pa can la yi dam 'cha' zhing spyod pa thams cad ni phyin ci log gi rgyu las byung ba ste/ de ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis thugs su chud de byin

112a3(phal chen): rtog par mi byed/ smon par mi byed/ chags par mi byed/ zhen par mi byed/ rten pani sems kyis gnas par mi byed de/ rmi lam gyi chos ngos bu don par byed kyang / dge ba'i rtsi nga 'di dag la snying ngan
112a4(phal chen): 'du shes mi skyed do/ / dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag la rten pa'i 'du shes su mi byed de/ 'on kyang rten pa'i sems can rnams gzud pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos kyang yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir brjod do//
112a5(phal chen): 'chad do// ston to// 'das pa'i chos la brtags na/ shar phyogs su rjes su mi mthong ngo // lho phyogs dang / nub phyogs dang / byang phyogs su rjes su mi mthong ngo // byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang /
112a6(phal chen): shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams dang / nub byang gi phyogs mtshams dang / 'og dang steng gi phyogs su rjes su mi mthong te/ de 'di snyam du gang ci yang rung ste/
112a7(phal chen): ma gtang ba de ni btang ba'o snyam du sems te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i 'das pa gtong ba'o// de la byang chub sems dpa'i ma 'ongs pa gtong ba gang zhe na/
112b1(phal chen): 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ma byon pa rnams kyi spyod pa nyan na/ mtshar ma'i tshul dang dngos por 'dzin pas mi 'dzin te/ 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan la brtson par
112b2(phal chen): mi byed pa yin/ tshol ba mi mnga' ba yin/ 'dod chags pa'i sems kyis mi smon pa yin/ de la sems mi sdud pa yin te/ myong bar mi byed do// smod par mi byed do// de dag tu dge ba'i
112b3(phal chen): rtsa ba rnams mi gtong ngo / / de dag tu dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams 'jug par mi byed de/ spyod pa yang rgyun gcod par mi byed do// 'on kyang dmigs pa des sangs rgyas kyi chos su 'grub par bya ba'i phyir
112b4(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang tshogs sdud par byed cing / chos nyid kyang rab tu sdud do// chos de ni yul na yang mi gnas/ phyogs na yang mi gnas/ nang na yang ma yin/ phyi rol na
112b5(phal chen): yang ma yin/ rgyang ring po na yang ma yin/ drung na'ang ma yin no zhes 'di snyam du sems te/ gang du nam yang spyad pa med par bya'o snyam pa 'di ni ma 'ongs pa gtong ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/
112b6(phal chen): de la byang chub sems dpa'i da ltar byung ba'i gtong ba gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' rgyal po chen po bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa
112b7(phal chen): gsum pa dang / mtshe ma dang / dga' ldan dang / 'phrul dga' dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed dang / tshangs pa dang / tshangs ris dang / tshangs lha nye phan dang /
113a1(phal chen): tshangs pa kun 'khor dang / tshangs chen dang / snang ba dang / 'od chung dang / tshad med snang ba dang / shin tu snang ba dang / dge ba dang / chung dge dang / tshad med dag pa dang / dge rgyas
113a2(phal chen): dang / che ba dang / chung che dang / tshad med che ba dang / 'bras bu che ba dang / mi che ba dang / mi gdung ba dang / shin tu mthong ba dang / gya nom snang ba dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams nas/ nyan thos kyi phun sum
113a3(phal chen): tshogs pa dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi phun sum tshogs pa dag kyang nyan te/ des de dag thos nas kyang rmongs par mi 'gyur/ shin tu rmongs par mi 'gyur/ rab tu rmongs par mi 'gyur/ zhum par mi 'gyur
113a4(phal chen): kun nas zhum par mi 'gyur/ rnam par zhum par mi 'gyur/ shin tu zhum par mi 'gyur/ dma' bar mi 'gyur te/ 'di ltar de ni shes pas 'du byed du gtogs pa thams cad rmi lam lta bur mngon du
113a5(phal chen): byed do/ / de ni 'di snyam du gang sbyin par bya ba 'di ni su'i yang ma yin no snyam ste/ ngan song gi lam nye bar gnas pa bzlog par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad bsgrub pa'i phyir chos ston kyang
113a6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i lam mngon du gyur pa'i phyir de la sems rgyu ba med de/ 'di ni de ltar byung ba gtong ba zhes bya'o// de la byang chub sems dpa'i shin tu gtong ba gang zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems
113a7(phal chen): dpa' sems can mig dang mi ldan pa dang / rna ba dang mi ldan pa dang / sna dang mi ldan pa dang / lce dang mi ldan pa dang / lus dang mi ldan pa grangs med pa zhig gis 'di skad du/ bdag cag la ci med pa de khyod kyis
113b1(phal chen): rgyan la/ red mi snyan pa med par byas shig/ myong ni bzhas pa mangs med par bskrun par 'dug cag ces zer/ byang chub sems dpa' na dathos sa thag tu sems can de dag mi ldan pa med par gyub /
113b2(phal chen): bskal pa grangs med par dbang po dang mi ldan pa de yang nyams su len to// de ma'i lto na 'dug pa'i tshe/ ji lta bur spyod pa dang / mer mer por 'dug pa ji lta bu yin pa dang / rdos par gyur pa ji lta bu yin pa dang /
113b3(phal chen): mkhregs par gyur pa ji lta bu yin pa dang / dbang po grub pa ji lta bu yin pa dang / skyes pa ji lta bu yin pa dang / rga ba ji lta bu yin pa dang / na ba ji lta bu yin pa dang / shi ba ji lta bu yin pa dang / lus kyi rang bzhin thog
113b4(phal chen): ma dang / bar dang / tha ma ji lta bu bzhin du yang dag par rab tu shes te/ ngom du mi rung ba/ ngo tsha skye ba/ 'phags pa ma yin pa/ dri mi zhim pa/ rjen pa'i dri can/ ror 'gyur ba/ rus pa sogs pa/ sha dang khrag gis
113b5(phal chen): g.yogs pa/ rma dgu nas rtag tu zag pa'o zhes nas/ de ni sems bskyed pa gcig tsam gyis kyang de don du gnyer bar mi sems te/ sems bskyed pa gcig gis kyang chags pa mi skyed do// de shin tu gtong ba des 'dzin pa med pa'i
113b6(phal chen): yid dang ldan pa yin te/ lus 'di ni de ltar snying po med pa yin na/ bdag gi lus 'di snying po med par mthong bzhin du lus la chags par ji ltar byas/ sems can 'di dag gi bsam pa de bzhin du yongs su chis par bya'o// lus
113b7(phal chen): snying po med pa 'dis 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsam pa yongs su rdzogs par bya'o/ / 'gro ba thams cad kyis kyang shes par bya'o// ye shes kyi tshogs gang yang rung ba la yang mi gnas pa'i tshul gyis gzhag par
114a1(phal chen): @#bya'o zhes nas/ lus kyi 'du shes kyang med/ sems kyi 'du shes med de/ kye rgyal ba'i sras pag/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i gtong ba'i gter te drug pa no/ kye rgyal ba
114a2(phal chen): sras dag/ de la byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi gter gang zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' gzugs rab tu shes so// gzugs kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so// gzugs kyi 'gog pa rab tu shes so// 5
114a3(phal chen): 'gog par 'gro ba'i lam yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so/ / de bzhin du tsho rab dang / 'du shes dang / 'du byed dang / rnam par shes pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so// rnam par shes pa kun 'byu

114a5(phal chen): so/ / ma rig pa rab tu shes so// ma rig pa'i kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so// ma rig pa 'gog pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so// ma rig pa 'gog par 'gyur ba'i lam yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du
114a6(phal chen): rab tu shes so/ / sred pa rab tu shes so// sred pa kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so// sred pa 'gog pa rab tu shes so// sred pa 'gog par 'gro ba'i lam yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so// nyan thos rab tu
114a7(phal chen): shes so/ / nyan thos kyi chos rab tu shes so// nyan thos kyi kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so// nyan thos kyi mya ngan las 'da' ba yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so// rang sangs rgyas rab tu shes so//
114b1(phal chen): rang sangs rgyas kyi chos rab tu shes so// rang sangs rgyas kyi kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so// rang sangs rgyas kyi yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so// byang chub sems dpa' rab
114b2(phal chen): tu shes so/ / byang chub sems dpa'i chos rab tu shes so// byang chub sems dpa'i kun 'byung ba rab tu shes so so// byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu dashe/
114b3(phal chen): so// ji ltar shes she na/ las dang / las kyi rnam par smin pa dang / bya ba dang / mngon par 'du byed pa dang / gsob dang / gsog dang / snying po med pa dang / bdag med pa rab tu shes te/ chos gang yang snying po can
114b4(phal chen): du shes pa med do/ / chos gang la yang rang bzhin du 'dogs pa med de/ ngo bo nyid kyi mthas gtugs par thams cad rab tu shes so// sems can rnams la yang de bzhin nyid kyi don du chos ston te/ de ci ston
114b5(phal chen): ce na/ 'jig pa med pa'i phyir chos ston te/ gang 'jig pa med pa'i phyir zhe na/ gzugs 'jig pa med pa'i phyir/ tshor ba 'jig pa med pa'i phyir/ 'du shes 'jig pa med pa'i phyir/ 'du byed 'jig pa med pa'i phyir/
114b6(phal chen): rnam par shes pa 'jig pa med pa'i phyir chos ston to// ma rig pa 'jig pa med pa'i phyir/ nyan thos kyi chos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi chos dang / byang chub sems dpa'i chos 'jig pa med pa'i phyir chos ston te//
114b7(phal chen): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ chos ni ma skyes pa/ 'dus ma byas pa/ byed pa po med pa rtsod pa med pa/ gnas pa med pa/ ma skyes pa/ mi 'byung ba/ ma blangs pa/ nye bar ma blangs pa
115a1(phal chen): byed pa med pa ste/ de shes rab kyi gter de lta bu dang ldan pas/ las glen chung ngus chos thams cad la mkhas pa gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so//
115a2(phal chen): shes rab kyi gter de yang mi zad pa yin te/ de yang shin tu bstan pa bcus mi zad pa yin no// bcu gang zhe na/ thos pa la mkhas pas mi zad do// dge ba'i bshes gnyen la bsnyen pas mi zad do// tshig rab tu
115a3(phal chen): dbye ba la mkhas pas mi zad do/ / chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa mngon par sgrub pas mi zad do// rgyan gcig pa'i ye shes kyi rjes su zhugs pas mi zad do// bsod nams thams cad shin tu bsags pas

130a5(phal chen): blta/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba shin tu dkon par ni rjes su sems shing / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ni rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa/ sgrib pa med pa'i chos can no zhes
130a6(phal chen): yang dag par blta zhing de logs su mngon par blta bar gyur to/ / dga' ldan gyi gnas na 'khod pa'i 'khor thams cad dang / lha bye ba brgya stong grangs med pa bcom ldan 'das ngasu ba'i phyir
130a7(phal chen): rin po che thams cad kyi me tog gi phur ma thogs thogs pa dang / spos thams cad kyi phur ma thogs thogs pa dang / rin po thams cad kyi phur ma thogs thogs pa dang / rgyan thams
130b1(phal chen): cad kyi phur ma thogs thogs pa dang / lha rdzas kyi tsan dan thams cad kyi phye ma'i phur ma thogs thogs pa dang / lha rdzas kyi a ka ru thams cad kyi phye ma'i phur ma thogs thogs pa dang / lha rdzas kyi
130b2(phal chen): rin po che thams cad kyi phye ma'i phur ma thogs thogs pa dang / lha rdzas kyi spos kyi me tog thams cad phye ma'i phur ma thogs thogs pa dang / lha rdzas kyi me tog man da ra ba'i phur ma thogs thogs pa rnams
130b3(phal chen): kyang dong ste/ bcom ldan 'das la gtor to// mngon par gtor to// rab tu gtor to// lha'i bu dga' ldan gyi gnas su gtogs pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa rnams kyang bar snang la 'khod de/
130b4(phal chen): ye shes kyi spyod yul la gzhol ba'i sems kyis spos dang bdug pa'i sprin gyis bdug pas bar snang brgyan pa byas so// sangs rgyas la dga' zhing gzhol ba'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi me tog thams cad kyi
130b5(phal chen): sprin gyi char gyis rab tu brgyan pas bar snang brgyan pa byas so/ / de bzhin gshegs pa la zhe sa cher bya ba'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi gdugs sna tshogs kyi sprin gyis bar yog par byas te brgyan pa byas so//
130b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas la mchod par gzhol ba'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi 'phreng ba sna tshogs kyi sprin rab tu bkye bas par snang brgyan byas so// sangs rgyas las thos par mos pa'i sems kyis gser gyi dra ba
130b7(phal chen): grangs med pa las dril bu sna tshogs kyi dra ba 'khrol zhing sgra 'byin pas yog par byas te bar snang brgyan pa byas so/ / de bzhin gshegs pa la yon gyi gnas dam pa yin par 'dzin pa'i sems kyis bla re
131a1(phal chen): grangs med pa las rin po che thams cad kyi semanar smin lding zhing 'phrul ba'i rgyan gyis bar snang brgyan pa byas so/ / sangs rgyas la dge bar 'dun pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi
131a2(phal chen): gzhal med khang grangs med par lha rdzas kyi rol mo brdung ba dang dkrol ba thams cad kyi sgra yid du 'ong ba phyung bas bar snang brgyan pa byas so/ / sangs rgyas skye ba shin tu dkon par dogs pa'i sems kyis
131a3(phal chen): lha rdzas kyi na bza' kha dog sna tshogs pa'i sprin dang na bza' mtshungs pa med pa'i sprin gyi char 'bab pa'i rgyan gyis bar snang brgyan pa byas so/ / sangs rgyas la mos pa mtha' yas pa'i sems kyis
131a4(phal chen): lha rdzas kyi cod pan grangs med pa'i sprin las cod pan gyi char chen po 'khor zhing 'bab pa'i rgyan gyis bar snang brgyan pa byas so/ / sangs rgyas la yid bde ba skyes pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi rin po
131a5(phal chen): che kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa'i sprin las 'phreng ba sna tshogs kyi char rgyun mi 'chad par 'bab pa'i rgyan gyis bar snang brgyan pa byas so/ / lha'i bu bye ba brgya stong grangs med pa yang lha rdzas kyi me tog
131a6(phal chen): kha dog tha dad pa grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ me tog zad mi shes pa'i mdzod rab tu bkye nas/ bcom ldan 'das la mngon par gtor to// mos pa'i spos dri zhim po rnyed cing sangs rgyas la dad par
131a7(phal chen): gnas pas/ lha rdzas kyi spos dang bdug pa kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ bcom ldan 'das la phul lo// rgyan chen po sprul pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi tsan ngan gyi phye ma
131b1(phal chen): kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ bcom ldan 'das la mngon par gtor to// dga' ba'i sems kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi zham ring du 'brang zhing rin po che'i gdugs kha dog sna
131b2(phal chen): tshogs grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ bcom ldan 'das la mngon par 'gebs so// sangs rgyas mtha' yas pa la mos pa'i sems rnam par 'phel bas gos rin po che kha dog sna tshogs grangs
131b3(phal chen): med pa lag na thogs te/ bcom ldan 'das gshegs pa'i lam gos kyis yog par byas so// de bzhin gshegs pa la rim gro bya bar mos pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi rgyal mtshan rin po che
131b4(phal chen): sna tshogs kyi kha dog can lag na thogs shing / bcom ldan 'das kyi zham ring du 'dong ngo // sangs rgyas la dga' ba mtha' yas pa rnam par 'phel ba'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi lha ba lbub dang byang
131b5(phal chen): phrul kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa'i yang grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la phul lo// dad pa mi 'phrogs pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi 'phreng ba grangs med pa lag na thogs
131b6(phal chen): te/ bcom ldan 'das la mngon par gtor to// mtshungs pa med pa'i dga' ba rnam par 'phel bas lha rdzas kyi ba dan rin po che kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa'i yang grangs med pa lag na thogs te/
131b7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das kyi drung nas 'dzin to// lha'i bu bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa yang zhi ba la rab tu gzhol zhing bag yod pa tshad med pa'i sems kyis/ lha rdzas kyi rol mo brdung ba dang
132a1(phal chen): dkrol ba kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa lagan thogs te/ yid du 'ong ba'i sgra dbyangs sbyang nas bcom ldan 'das dgyes par byed do// byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag
132a2(phal chen): khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa dga' ldan gyi gnas nas 'ongs pa'i rnams kyang / lha rdzas las 'das pa'i mchod pa khams gsum las rnam par 'das la/ dmigs pa'i chos las byung ba
132a3(phal chen): rjen pa'i dri med pa/ chags pa med pa'i sems tshim par byed pa/ chos kyi tshul zab mos mngon par grub pa/ blo tshad med par yangs pa las byung ba/ dad pa'i rtsa ba brtan pas rnam par spel ba/
132a4(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa las byung ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba dang 'phrul pa grangs med pas mngon par bsgrubs pa/ sangs rgyas mchod pa yid kyi rang bzhin las byung ba/ mngon par 'du bya ba med pa'i
132a5(phal chen): chos kyi sgo'i rgyas btab pas/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad kun nas yog par byas so// lha rdzas las 'das pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa las byung ba'i me tog gi bla re sna tshogs kyis chos kyi dbyings kun nas
132a6(phal chen): khebs par byas so/ / lha rdzas las 'das pa mos pas rnam par dag pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul rgyas par 'gengs pa'i na bza' sna tshogs mngon par dgab pas chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas
132a7(phal chen): so/ / chags pa med pa'i chos kyi rang bzhin rdo rje la yang dag par zhugs pa'i sems kyis/ lha rdzas las 'das pas mi skye ba'i chos las byung ba'i dril bu tshom bur bcad pa'i dra bas chos kyi dbyings brgyan
132b1(phal chen): pa byas so/ / chos thams cad sgyu ma lta bur rtogs pa'i sems kyis/ lha rdzas las 'das pa'i spros thams cad kyi mchog gis bdug pa'i rgyan gyis chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so// de bzhin gshegs
132b2(phal chen): pa bzhugs pas chos kyi dbyings rgyas par bya ba'i sems kyis/ lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che thams cad kyi khri sangs rgyas kyi gdan du bting ba'i rgyan gyis chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so//
132b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi mchod pa rang bzhin 'gag pa med pa'i sems kyis/ lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgyal mtshan yang dag par bsgreng ba'i rgyan gyis chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so//
132b4(phal chen): rmi lam lta bu'i chos nyid kyis bsam pa tshim pas/ lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che sna tshogs kyis sangs rgyas kyi pho brang brgyan pas chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so// mi gnas pa'i dge ba'i rtsa
132b5(phal chen): ba blang ba med pa las byung bas/ lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che sna tshogs kyi pad+mos kun nas yog pa'i rgyan gyis chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so// lha rdzas las 'das pa'i spros thams cad kyi
132b6(phal chen): / mchog gi sprin gyis chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par bya ba dang / me tog kha dog mtha' yas pa sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / na bza' kha dog sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad pa thams cad kyi sprin dang /
132b7(phal chen): dan gyi dri zhim po mtha' yas par 'pho ba thams cad kyi sprin dang / lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che thams cad kyi gdugs rnam pa sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / spos dang bdug pa sna tshogs kyi ngang kun
133a1(phal chen): ldang ba'i sprin dang / 'phreng ba yid du 'ong ba thams cad kyi sprin dang / lha rdzas las 'das pa'i lhab lhub rnam par dag pa thams cad kyi sprin dang / byang chub sems dpa' bye ba
133a2(phal chen): khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa rang gi lus gtong ba'i sprin dang / sangs rgyas kyi yon tan brjod pa las 'das pas bstod cing bsngags pa'i brjod pa zad mi shes pa'i sprin dang / de bzhin gshegs
133a3(phal chen): pa'i bstod pas brjod pa ji lta ba bzhin du yang dag par bsngags pa'i chos ma log pa las byung ba sangs rgyas kyi stobs mtha' dang dbus med pa las rgyu bas/ 'gro ba thams cad bde ba'i lam bstan pa dang /
133a4(phal chen): tshig rnam par 'byed pa brjod du med pa smos pas/ chos tshad med pa la gzhol ba'i gzungs kyi rgyud thams cad las byung ba'i so so yang dag par rig pa la mkhas pa/ mi zad pa dang mi 'jigs pa'i yid
133a5(phal chen): dga' bar gyur pa'i rim gro ngoms mi shes pas de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par bstod pa/ tshig rnam par dbye zhing brjod pas byang chub sems dpa' de dag chos kyi dbyings kyi lus nam mkha'i khams
133a6(phal chen): rgyas par byed pa byin gyis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba thams cad kyis yongs su bzung ba'i yid kyi dbang pos mngon par bstod do// lha'i ris
133a7(phal chen): gzhan dang gzhan nas 'dus pa'i lha'i 'khor de dag thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa nas 'dus pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor rnams kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa
133b1(phal chen): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongs su ston cing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku yang dag par 'byung ba dang / bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rdzu
133b2(phal chen): 'phrul yang dag par ston pa dang / sems can grangs med pa'i rgyud tshim par mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rgyan rnam par phye bas nam mkha'i khams thams cad dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad

133b7(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rigs rgyun mi gcod pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa mtha' dang dbus med pa 'byung ba brnyes pa/ 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams

149b4(phal chen): pa ma yin te/ / ma 'ongs pa yang ska ma yin// skyes dang byang chub mya ngan 'das// skad cig gis ni rab tu snang // ji ltar sgyu mar gyur pa'i gzugs// skyes pa ma yin 'ongs pa min// de ltar
149b5(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku/ / skye ba med par shin tu bstan// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rin po che'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcur
149b6(phal chen): rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// yang dag sangs rgyas tshad med pas// tshad du sku yang rnam par bstan// ji ltar 'dul ba'i sems can rnams// de bzhin
149b7(phal chen): 'dren pa rab tu mthong / / sku la phyogs ni med par brjod// sangs rgyas yul ni ma lus khyab// bar snang nam mkha' ji lta bar// de bzhin sangs rgyas bsam mi khyab// der ni sems kyang
150a1(phal chen): 'pho ba med/ / sems la skye ba yod la'ang min// sangs rgyas rnams kyi spyod yul ni// skye ba med la rab tu gnas// ji ltar rab rib ldan pa'i mig/ nang na'ang med cing
150a2(phal chen): phyina'ang med/ / de bzhin 'jig rten sangs rgyas dag/ nang na'ang mi bzhugs phyi na'ang min// 'jig rten kun gyi don gyi phyir// rkang gnyis kyi ni mchog byung ste// 'jig rten du ni ma byung yang //
150a3(phal chen): 'jig rten dag tu skye bos mthong // sangs rgyas rnams la zhing mi gnas// rgyal ba dag la nyin mtshan med// skad cig ma yin zla ba min// rgyal ba la ni lo mi gnas// 'jig rten dag na 'di skad brjod// /
150a4(phal chen): nyi ma che ge mo zhig tu// rang byung byang chub rgyal bas thob// sangs rgyas nyi ma'i rjes mi 'brang // de la bskal pa yod ma yin// dus kyang ma lus med pa ste// dus gsum yang dag rdzogs sangs rgyas// /
150a5(phal chen): mgon po rnams ni mnga' bar 'gyur// ji ltar nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor ni// nams kyang mtshan dang mi gnas te// nyin mtshan zhes kyang rab tu brjod// de bzhin sangs rgyas chos nyid do// bskal pa
150a6(phal chen): gcig dang dus gsum du/ / 'dren pa bzhugs pa ma yin te// dus gsum zhes kyang rab tu brjod// sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos nyid ltos// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdul
150a7(phal chen): dang bral ba'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// yang dag sangs rgyas sku gcig ste/
150b1(phal chen): 'dren pa thams cad don gcig kyang // tshad med gzhan dang gzhan dag tu// phyogs bcu kun na rab tu snang // gang gis ma lus thams cad kyi// chos kyi dbyings rnams kun khyab pa// sems
150b2(phal chen): can gtso bo thub pa yi/ / spyod yul rnams ni ci 'dra ltos// sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos nyid ni// nang gi skus kyang snang ba min// de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs// phyi rol skus kyang mi
150b3(phal chen): snang ngo / / dus mang kun tu las rnams kyis// ji ltar las rnams bsags pa bzhin// de bzhin so sor phye ba'i skus// rigs su byung ba rab tu bstan// rgyal ba'i chos nyid ma gtogs par//
150b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas sku ni 'di 'dra ba// grangs su bgrang bar mi nus te// bsams pas lta yang shes mi nus// ji ltar bdag cag sems kyi las// bsam gyis mi khyab mi 'byung ba// de bzhin sangs
150b5(phal chen): rgyas bsam mi khyab/ / sems kyi 'phrin las mi mnga' 'o// ji ltar zhing rnams bsam yas pa// sa la rnam par dag pas mdzes// de bzhin sangs rgyas bsam mi khyab// 'gro ba dag na mdzes
150b6(phal chen): par snang / / ji ltar las rnams 'jug pa ni// rkyen gyis rab tu 'byung 'gyur ba// de bzhin rgyu rnams 'thun pa las// sangs rgyas shin tu mthong bar 'gyur// yid bzhin nor bu'i rgyal po ni// ji
150b7(phal chen): ltar yid bsams rdzogs byed pa/ / de bzhin sangs rgyas chos nyid kyang // rtag tu smon lam rdzogs par sgrub// mtha' dang dbus med 'jig rten 'dir// 'jig rten mgon po 'dren par gyur
151a1(phal chen): de yi smon lam de dag gis/ / phyogs bcu 'di dag rgyal bas gang // de nas byang chub sems dpa' dri ma med pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis
151a2(phal chen): brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// ye shes dkyil 'khor sangs rgyas te// 'jig rten chos rnams rnam par sbyong // 'jig rten chos
151a3(phal chen): rnams rnam sbyangs nas/ / sangs rgyas chos rnams rab tu brjod// de ste sems can mnyam sangs rgyas// sems can la las bsam byas na// rgyal ba de dag thams cad mthong // sangs rgyas la
151a4(phal chen): ni gshegs pa med/ / sangs rgyas la ni dmigs byas nas// sems kyis sangs rgyas dmigs pas na// sems bskyed pa dang rgyal mnyam par// de bzhin de dag rgyal ba mthong // dkar ba'i chos kyis
151a5(phal chen): nyer brtan cing / / gang gis grags pa rnam sbyangs pa// de dag thams cad sems bskyed la// shes rab ldan pa rab tu bzhugs// dmigs pa dag dang byin gyis brlabs// mi yi gtso bo ston pa mdzad/
151a6(phal chen): de phyir dmigs pa kun tu yang // sangs rgyas rgyal ba gshegs par brjod// 'jig rten khams rnams 'di dag ni// sangs rgyas sku rnams bdag gi med// sems la bdag gi med pa bstan// byang chub
151a7(phal chen): rtogs la bdag gi med/ / mi yi se ge'i chos nyid dang // dpa' ba'i stobs la rab tu gnas// lus dang mtshan nyid mi 'dra ste// snang ba'i sems dang mnyam pa'i sku// ji ltar 'jig rten de bzhin sku// ji bzhin
151b1(phal chen): / skur yang rgyal ba ste// sku yi rang bzhin shes pa ni// sangs rgyas chags pa med ces bya// sangs rgyas kun tu gzigs pa ste// chos rnams thams cad rab tu gzigs// sangs rgyas chos dang byang chub
151b2(phal chen): rnams/ / gang la'ang dmigs pa med pa yin// sangs rgyas la ni gshegs pa med// sangs rgyas gang na'ang mi bzhugs te// yang dag sangs rgyas log pa med// de bzhin gshegs la len mi mnga'//
151b3(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa' dpal gyi rgyal mtshan gyis// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// sangs
151b4(phal chen): rgyas thams cad kun tu khyab/ / zhing gcig la ni mi gnas te// thams cad du ni sangs rgyas gshegs// zhing rnams kun tu rab tu snang // sangs rgyas sku ni thams cad du// byin gyis brlabs dag rab tu 'byung // 'tshang rgya
151b5(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo dang / / bsam pa bzhin du mya ngan 'da'// sangs rgyas la ni su zhig sems// ci phyir sangs rgyas bsam mi khyab// yang dag sangs rgyas su yis mthong // rgyal ba sus kyang mthong bar 'gyur// ji ltar chos
151b6(phal chen): rnams chos nyid dang / / ji ltar sangs rgyas spyod yul du// gang dag chos rnams gcig tsam yang // de bzhin nyid la mi 'jug go// 'di ni 'jig rten 'di rgyal zhes// 'jig rten dag na rnam rtog yod// gang gis ngo bo nyid
151b7(phal chen): shes na/ / 'jig rten med de rgyal ba'ang med// 'jig rten dad par bya ba'i phyir// mgon po dag ni mngon sum ston// de dag gi ni blta ba 'di// shin tu dmigs par mi rung ngo // gang gis chags pa rnam pa zlog cing // chags/
152a1(phal chen): ma med la dga' byed pa// chags pa thams cad rnam bzlog nas// chags med chos nyid rtogs par 'gyur// sangs rgyas zhes brjod gang yin dang // gang gis rnam 'phrul snang 'gyur ba'i/
152a2(phal chen): chos ni dus gsum thams cad du// rnam pa kun tu mi rnyed do// gang gis chos nyid 'di shes shing // gang gis 'di bzhin yid ches na// thams cad mkhyen cing kun gzigs pa'i/ de bzhin gshegs par myur du
152a3(phal chen): 'gyur/ / sangs rgyas thams cad rnam 'phrul pa// 'di dag thams cad tshig gis bstan// yang dag sangs rgyas tshig lam med// tshig gi lam gyis rab tu brjod// de nas byang chub sems
152a4(phal chen): dpa' chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// gang gis rnam par 'phrul snang ba'i// sangs rgyas
152a5(phal chen): mthong ba med pa bas/ / 'jig rten khams rnams thams cad kyi// sdug bsngal phung po blangs kyang bla// 'gro ba gang gis byang chub tu// sems ni nam yang ma bskyed pa// de dag gnas 'di thos gyur
152a6(phal chen): na/ sangs rgyas byang chub 'grub par 'gyur// gang gis bsam pa gcig gis kyang // 'di la mos byed mkhas pa ni// mi yi mchog tu mi 'gyur zhes// des ni the tshom mi bya'o// de yi rnam par
152a7(phal chen): 'phrul pa ni/ / bskal pa bye ba'i bar du dkon// su zhig 'di la mos byed pa// de dag bla na med par 'gyur// brjod du med pa'i sangs rgyas rnams// skad cig skad cig bsnyen bkur yang /
152b1(phal chen): 'di yi tshul la mi gnas na// de dag bsnyen bkur byas ma yin// gang la sangs rgyas brjod gyur pa'i// chos 'di gang gis thos gyur pa// des ni mi bde kun gyis kyang // spyad pa rnams ni blang bar bya//
152b2(phal chen): ji tsam chos kyi dbyings rnams dang // dus gsum gyi ni mgon po yi// sangs rgyas rnams ni rten pa yi// ye shes chen po gcig thos nas// phyi mtha'i bskal pa bye ba rnams// zhing rnams re
152b3(phal chen): rer zad byas shing / / 'di yi tshul ni brtson byed na// de la byang chub dkon pa med// sems can rnams kyi sngon mtha' yi// 'khor bar mi rnams gnas gyur kyang // des ni sangs rgyas rab byung ba// /
152b4(phal chen): chos nyid 'di ni shes ma gyur// chos rnams zhig par byas pa med// chos ni 'jig par mi 'gyur te// kun tu snang las rnam 'phrul pa// 'jig rten de dag thams cad bstan// shin tu rgyas pa chen
152b5(phal chen): bopo'i mdo sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ dga' ldan gyi gnas su byang chub sems dpa' 'dus pa'i tshigs su bcad pa bstan pa'i le'u ste nyi shu dgu pa'o// // de nas
152b6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan de'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus ting nge 'dzin ye shes snang ba zhes bya ba la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan byang chub
152b7(phal chen): sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ye shes snang ba zhes bya ba de la snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu/ de'i tshe na phyogs bcu'i phyogs re rer 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
153a1(phal chen): 'das pa'i pha rol na/ de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcwa phrag stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba sbed kyis zhal bstan pa mthong ste/ de dag kyang 'di lta ste/ mtshan rdorje
153a2(phal chen): rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba sha stag go/ / phyogs gcig nas ji lta ba de ltar/ phyogs bcu nas kyang de bzhin te/ de la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis 'di skad ces kyang bka' stsal to// rdo rje'i rgyal
153a3(phal chen): mtshan de ltar khyod byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ye shes snang ba la snyoms par zhugs pa legs so lags so/ / 'di ltar yang rigs kyi bu khyod la phyogs bcu nas de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas
153a4(phal chen): kyi zhing brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed thams cad kyang mtshan 'thun pa sha sag gis/ 'di ltar bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad 'di'i sngon gyi smon lam dang / sngon gyi byin gyis brlabs
153a5(phal chen): dang / khyod kyi ye shes rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa bas brtan pa'i phyir 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i mi 'jigs pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang / spobs pa chags pa
153a6(phal chen): med par bya ba dang / ye shes kyis bsgribs pa med pa'i sar 'jug par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems yangs pa la rab tu 'jug par bya ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba mi zad pa phun sum tshogs par bya ba
153a7(phal chen): dang / bsgribs pa med pa'i chos dkar po yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings la sgo kun nas 'jug par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi cho 'phrul bstan par bya ba dang / sngon gyi mtha'i mur
153b1(phal chen): thug pa'i ye shes dang dran pa rgyun mi chod pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang / dbang po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis byin du brlab par bya ba dang / chos kyi sgo mtha' yas la bstan par bya ba dang /
153b2(phal chen): shes pa kun gzung bar bya ba dang / 'di lta ste/ yongs su bsngo ba bcu yongs su rdzogs par bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba gzung bar bya ba dang / 'jig rten las 'das
153b3(phal chen): pa'i tshogs rnams rab tu bstan par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes mi chod par bya ba dang / smon lam chen po'i skabs dbye bar bya ba dang / don shin tu bstan pa la 'jug pa bya ba dang / chos
153b4(phal chen): kyi dbyings yongs su shes par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi yid rab tu dga' bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi srid pa gsum gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba 'thun pa la brten par bya ba dang /
153b5(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs yang dag par gzung bar bya ba'i phyir byin gyis brlabs pa mdzad kyis/ kye rigs kyi bu khyod kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyis byin
153b6(phal chen): gyis brlabs pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bsod nams kyis brtan pa dang / gzungs kyi snang ba la zhugs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos bsgribs pa med pa la zhugs pa dang / chos kyi
153b7(phal chen): dbyings snang ba'i chos nyid du bya ba dang / kha na ma tho ba med pa'i chos dkar po yang dag par bsgrub par bya ba dang / ye shes kyi spyod yul yangs pa la gnas pa dang / bsgribs pa med pa'i chos snang
154a1(phal chen): ba la gnas pas chos bstan pa 'di brjod pa dang bstan pa'i phyir spobs par gyis shig/ de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyi
154a2(phal chen): ye shes tshad med pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ / spobs pa chags pa med pa dang tshig rab tu dbye ba la mkhas pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// bsgribs pa med pa'i chos kyi snang ba nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do//
154a3(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sku dang gcig pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// tshad med pa'i dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin bsam gyis
154a4(phal chen): mi khyab pa rnam par dbye ba la mkhas pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad nyams pa med par yongs su bsngo ba'i ye shes nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// chos thams cad kyi lhag
154a5(phal chen): mthong mngon par bskyed pa la mkhas pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ / chos thams cad bstan pa'i gnas rgyun mi chod pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar ting nge 'dzin 'di nyid kyi dge ba'i
154a6(phal chen): rtsa ba'i gzi brjid kyi phyir ro/ / de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis phyag g.yas pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyi spyi bo la byug pa mdzad do// sangs
154a7(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan la reg ma thag tu ting nge 'dzin de las rnam par langs te/ langs nas kyang byang chub sems dpa' de dag la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i
154b1(phal chen): sras dag/ byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam 'di lta ste/ 'gro ba thams cad khyab par byed pa/ sems can thams cad yongs su skyob pa 'di ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la gnas
154b2(phal chen): shing byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba la slob bo/ / ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yongs
154b3(phal chen): su bsngo ba la slob par 'gyur ro/ / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba la slob bo// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi yongs
154b4(phal chen): su bsngo ba gang la bsams te de skad du smras pa de dag ni gang / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ yongs su bsngo ba'i grangs ni du zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ bsngo ba bcu po 'di dag ni 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang /
154b5(phal chen): da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsungs so// gsung ngo // gsung bar 'gyur ro// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sems can rnams kyi 'du shes 'gog cing 'gro ba thams cad yongs su
154b6(phal chen): skyob pa zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba dang po dang / mi phyed pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba gnyis pa dang / sangs rgyas thams
154b7(phal chen): cad la yang dag par bskyed pa zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba gsum pa dang / thams cad du rjes su song ba zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba bzhi pa dang
155a1(phal chen): bsod nams kyi mdzod mi zad pa zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba lnga pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ba zhes bya ba/
155a2(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba drug pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ba zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba 'dun pa dang / de bzhin
155a3(phal chen): gshegs pa'i mtshan nyid kyi rang bzhin zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba brgyad pa dang / chags pa med cing bcings pa dang bkrol ba med pa zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'
155a4(phal chen): rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba dgu pa dang / chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa'i rjes su song ba zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang chub sems
155a5(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba bcu po de dag ni 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsungs so// gsung ngo // gsung bar 'gyur ro//

155a7(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la rab tu sbyor ba 'am/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la rnam par sbyong ba 'am/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la sems
155b1(phal chen): pa 'am/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la rtsom pa 'am/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la rnam par dpyod pa 'am/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la 'jug pa 'am/ byams pa bsgom pa yang dag
155b2(phal chen): par bskyed pa 'am/ snying rjes snying brtse bar byed pa 'am/ dga' ba la rab tu dga' bar byed pa 'am/ btang snyoms la shin tu gnas pa byed kyang rung ste/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la shin tu bsams nas/
155b3(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba de dang de dag la rab tu sbyor zhing dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa rnam par phye nas/ 'di ltar dge ba'i rtsa ba gang gis sems can rnams kyi sems can dmyal ba'i ngan song rgyun 'chad par 'gyur
155b4(phal chen): ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang gshin rje'i 'jig rten pa rnams kyi sdug bsngal gyi phung po rnam par ldog par 'gyur ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba 'gro ba thams cad la rnam pa dag pa'i mthar phyin par phan 'dogs
155b5(phal chen): pa gang yin zhes sems bskyed do/ / de de ltar dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yang dag par bskyed pa na 'di ltar yongs su bsngo ste/ dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis sdug bsngal gyi phung po thams cad rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/
155b6(phal chen): bdag sems can thams cad kyi gnas su gyur cig/ nyon mongs pa thams cad las yongs su dgrol ba'i phyir/ bdag sems can thams cad kyi dpung gnyen du gyur cig/ 'jigs pa kun las
155b7(phal chen): bsrung ba'i phyir/ bdag sems can thams cad kyi skyabs su gyur cig/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i sa thob par bya ba'i phyir/ bdag sems can thams cad kyi lam du gyur cig/ shin tu bde ba dang ldan
156a1(phal chen): pa 'thob par bya ba'i phyir/ bdag sems can thams cad kyi rten du gyur cig/ rab rib med pa ye shes snang ba yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir/ bdag sems can thams cad
156a2(phal chen): kyi sdang bar gyur cig/ ma rig pa'i mun pa rnam par bsal ba'i phyir/ bdag sems can thams cad kyi sgron mar gyur cig/ shin tu dag pa la rab tu dgod pa'i phyir/ bdag sems can thams
156a3(phal chen): cad kyi mar mer gyur cig/ chos kyi tshul la gzud pa'i phyir/ bdag sems can thams cad kyi 'dren par gyur cig/ bsgribs pa med pa'i ye shes kyi phung po bstabs pa'i phyir/ bdag
156a4(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi yongs su 'dzin par gyur cig ces/ de de ltar 'grob thams cad kyi don du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mthar shin tu thug par dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yongs su bsdu ste/
156a5(phal chen): ltar mdza' ba bsrung ba'i phyir/ yongs su bsngo ba de ltar mi mdza' ba bsrung ba'i phyir yang yongs su bsngo'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams la bdag tu bya ba'i
156a6(phal chen): bsam pas mi mdza' ba ni gang yang med de/ de yang 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' ni chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid la yang dag par byung ba ste/ de 'di snyam du byang chub sems dpa' mi mdza' ba'i don byed
156a7(phal chen): pa de dag thams cad ni bdag gi rgyud la dgod dgod pa yin no zhes te/ de dag ni sems can thams cad kyi yul thams cad la zhe sdang ba med pa'i mig gis blta'o// byang chub sems dpa' sems
156b1(phal chen): dpa' chen po rnams ni 'gro ba thams cad kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen te/ sems can thams cad la dge ba'i chos yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir 'jug go// 'di lta ste/ dper na rgya mtsho chen po ni dug thams cad
156b2(phal chen): kyis gdug par bya bar mi nus so/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang drin mi gzo ba dang / blo zhan pa dang / sems 'khrugs pa dang / rnyog pa dang / mun par gyur pa dang / rang bzhin stor ba dang
156b3(phal chen): rlom sems dang ldan pa dang / sgrubs pa nyams pa dang / sems dmus long lta bur gyur pa'i sems can byis pa thams cad kyis skyon can du mi nus so// 'di lta ste/ dper na lha'i bu nyi ma 'char ba de ni
156b4(phal chen): dmus long gi skyon gyis 'char ba las thogs par mi 'gyur ro/ / dri za'i grong khyer gyi skyon gyis thogs par mi 'gyur ro// gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sa'i rdul gyi skyon gyis thogs par mi 'gyur ro// /
156b5(phal chen): lha ma yin gyi dbang po sgra gcan gyi skyon gyis thogs par mi 'gyur ro// du ba 'khrigs pa'i skyon gyis thogs par mi 'gyur ro// 'dzam bu'i gling gi nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i skyon gyis thogs par mi 'gyur ro// /
156b6(phal chen): grib ma sna tshogs kyi skyon gyis thogs par mi 'gyur ro// dug gi ri'i skyon gyis thogs par mi 'gyur ro// khams kyi nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i skyon gyis thogs par mi 'gyur ro// dus yongs su 'gyur ba'i
156b7(phal chen): skyon gyis thogs par mi 'gyur ro/ / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dran pa can yang dag par shes pa dang ldan pa/ sems kyi bdag nyid che ba nyid shin tu zab cing yangs la
157a1(phal chen): yid la yang dag par rtog pa mi zhan pa/ yon tan spyad pas ye shes kyi mthar gyur pa/ chos la shin tu dad pa'i sems mngon par skyes pa/ chos kyi snang ba'i 'od kyis rab
157a2(phal chen): tu snang ba/ don thams cad mthong ba/ chos mngon par shes pa/ ye shes rig pa rtsod pa med pa lhur byed pa/ sems can thams cad dge ba'i chos spyod pa la rab tu sbyor ba/ sems can thams
157a3(phal chen): cad kyis nyes par sems bskyed pa la 'khrul pa med pa de yang dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yongs su bsngo ba na/ gnod par byed pa thams cad kyi skyon gyis thogs par mi 'gyur ro// sems can mi bsrun
157a4(phal chen): pa'i tshul gyis ldog par mi 'gyur ro/ / sems can gyi lta ba'i rnyog pas dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bsngo ba dang 'bral bar mi 'gyur ro// sems can gyi sems 'khrug pas ldog par mi 'gyur ro// sems can
157a5(phal chen): kyi sems kyi rgyud stor bas byang chub sems dpa'i go cha chen po bgos pa las ring bar mi 'gyur ro/ / 'gro ba thams cad yongs su bskyab pa'i smon lam dkrugs ma'i rnyog pa thams cad kyis
157a6(phal chen): bcil bar mi 'gyur ro/ / byang chub sems dpa'i rtsom pa chen po sems can drin du mig zo ba mthong bas lhod par mi 'gyur ro// byang chub tu dmigs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba sems can mi bsrun pa'i dbang pos
157a7(phal chen): zhub par mi 'gyur ro/ / dge ba'i rtsa ba ji lta ba bzhin las byis pa'i skye bo dang 'grogs pa las 'phang bar mi 'gyur ro// sems can gzhan gyi skyon gyis skyo bar mi 'gyur ro// /
157b1(phal chen): shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdobs po sum su ca gnyis pa/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ dkyil 'khor 'di ni bsgribs pa med par 'gro ba thams cad rnam par dag par bya ba'i
157b2(phal chen): phyir 'byung ba ste/ sems can gcig la dmigs shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bsngo ba ma yin/ 'di lta ste/
157b3(phal chen): zhing rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir zhing gcig la dmigs te/ byang chub sems dpa' byang chub kyi sems la mngon par spro ba ma yin/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas blta ba rnam par dmigs pa'i
157b4(phal chen): phyir sangs rgyas gcig la dmigs te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dad pa skye ba ma yin/ 'di lta ste/ ye shes gcig rjes su rtogs pa'i phyir ye shes gcig la dmigs nas/
157b5(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi smon lam skye ba ma yin gyi/ 'di ltar sems can thams cad yongs su skyab pa'i phyir dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams yongs su bsngo'o// zhing thams cad yongs
157b6(phal chen): su sbyang ba'i phyir dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams yongs su bsngo'o/ / sangs rgyas thams cad la mchod cing rim gro bya ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas thams cad blta ba la dmigs nas byang chub sems
157b7(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi dad pa skye'o/ / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi ye shes kyis rjes su rtogs par bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bla na med pa yang dag par
158a1(phal chen): rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su sngo ba rnams kyi smon lam skye'o/ / de yang 'di lhur byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sangs rgyas kyi
158a2(phal chen): stobs la dmigs pa la sems yangs pa/ bsam pa ma 'khums pa/ bskal pa thams cad du shin tu dkon pa'i sems rin po che dang ldan pa rnams kyi sems ni 'di lta ste/
158a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir rab tu skyes te/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yang dag par mthong nas/ sems dad pa
158a4(phal chen): chen po rnam par dag pa dang / snying rje chen pos brtan pas bsngo zhing dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag sems can thams cad la yongs su bsngo ste/ de yang tshig tsam du ma yin gyi/ bsam pa thag
158a5(phal chen): pas yongs su bsngo'o/ / de yang dga' ba'i sems dang / rab tu dga' ba'i sems dang / dad pa'i sems dang / mos pa'i sems dang / 'jam pa'i sems dang / byams pa'i sems dang //
158a6(phal chen): nye ba'i sems dang / snying rtse ba'i sems dang / phan gdags pa'i sems kyis yongs su bsngo'o// de yang 'di ltar yongs su bsngo ste/ bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis sems can thams cad
158a7(phal chen): kyi 'gro ba rnam par dag par gyur cig/ skye ba yongs su dag par gyur cig/ bsod nams kyi bdag nyid che ba yongs su rdzogs par gyur cig/ zil gyis mi non par gyur cig/ mi zad par
158b1(phal chen): gyur cig/ thub par dka' ba'i sems su gyur cig/ dran pa nyams pa med par gyur cig/ rtogs pa nges par gyur cig/ blo tshad med par gyur cig/ lus kyi las dang / ngag gi las dang
158b2(phal chen): yid kyi las kyi yon tan gyi rgyan thams cad yongs su rdzogs par gyur cig/ dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis sems can de dag thams cad sangs rgyas thams cad mnyes par byed par gyur cig/ ma zhes
158b3(phal chen): par byas nas kyang thugs 'byung ba med par gyur cig/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag la mi phyed pa'i dad pa yang thob par gyur cig/ de dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag
158b4(phal chen): par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis chos bstan pa thob par gyur cig/ thos nas kyang the tshom dang yid gnyis med par gyur cig/ yang dag par 'dzin cing nan tan gyis sgrub par gyur cig/
158b5(phal chen): sems kyi dga' ba nyid kyang thob par gyur cig/ kha na ma tho ba med pa'i lus kyi las kyang yang dag par grub par gyur cig/ dge ba'i rtsa ba chen po la bdag rab tu gzhog par gyur cig/ shin tu
158b6(phal chen): dbul ba dang rnam par bral bar gyur cig/ nor bdun thob pa yongs su rdzogs par gyur cig/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su yang slob par gyur cig/ dge ba'i dbang po thob par bya ba yang
158b7(phal chen): thob par gyur cig/ mos pa chen po'i mnyam pa nyid kyang yongs su rdzogs par gyur cig/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi go yang rnyed par gyur cig/ 'gro ba thams cad du nyams pa med pa'i
159a1(phal chen): mig kyang skyed par gyur cig/ mtshan gyis 'argyan pa'i lus yongs su rdzogs pa yang thob par gyur cig/ yon tan thams cad kyis brgyan pa'i tshig rnam par dag pa yang
159a2(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs par gyur cig/ dbang po bsdams shing stobs bcu dang ldan pa'i sems dge ba yang yang dag par grub par gyur cig/ gnas med par spyod pa yang yongs su rdzogs
159a3(phal chen): par gyur cig/ sangs rgyas thams cad bde ba'i rim gro gang dang ldan pa'i bde ba'i rim gro de dag sems can thams cad kyis thob par gyur cig/ sangs rgyas kyi gnas rab tu thob
159a4(phal chen): pas tshad med pa'i gnas su gyur cig/ sems can de dag thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi phung po sgrib pa'i las sna tshogs las byung ba sgrib pa'i las de dag gis bsgribs pas sangs rgyas
159a5(phal chen): mi mthong ba dang / chos mi thos pa dang / dge 'dun mi shes pa'i bsgribs pa'i las rnam pa sna tshogs kyis bsags pa'i sdug bsngal gyi phung po de dag bdag gi lus 'dis sems can dmyal
159a6(phal chen): ba'i skye gnas dang / ngan song gi sa'i gnas de dang de dag tu blang bar bya'o// sems can de dag thams cad ni dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis de nas bton te/ bdag gis de dag gi sdug bsngal dang
159a7(phal chen): nyon mongs pa de dag blang bar bya'o/ / spro bar bya'o// mi ldog par bya'o// de las mi 'bros par bya'o// mi skrag par bya'o// mi 'jigs par bya'o// phyir mi ldog par bya'o// zhum pa med
159b1(phal chen): par bya'o/ / mi skyo bar bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bdag gis ni sems can thams cad bsgral bar smon lam btab pas na sems can thams cad kyi khur bskur dgos so// 'di ltar
159b2(phal chen): bdag gis sems can thams cad yongs su dgrol bar bya'o/ / 'di ltar bdag gis sems can thams cad bsgral bar bya'o// skye ba'i dgon pa dang / rga ba dang na ba'i dgon pa dang
159b3(phal chen): 'chi ba'i dgon pa dang / 'chi 'pho dang skye ba'i dgon pa dang / nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi dgon pa dang / mi khom pa thams cad kyi dgon pa dang / 'khor ba thams cad kyi dgon pa dang
159b4(phal chen): lta ba thibs po thams cad kyi dgon pa dang / dge ba'i chos thams cad stor ba'i dgon pa dang / mi shes pa las byung ba'i dgon pa dang / dgon pa de dag thams cad nas bdag gis sems
159b5(phal chen): can sred pa'i dra bas 'khrigs pa dang / ma rig pa'i sgrib pas bsgribs pa srid pa'i sred pa dang ldan pa/ zhen pa'i mthar gyur pa dang / sdug bsngal gyi shing tags kyis bskor ba/
159b6(phal chen): bdud kyi las la rten pa/ mi mkhas la/ bsod nams 'gags pa/ the tsom du gyur pa/ rtag tu yid gnyis dang ldan pa/ mi bde ba mthong ba/ 'byung ba la mi mkhas pa/ tshub ma'i
159b7(phal chen): bskor ba'i lo ma lta bur 'khor zhing 'phyan pa de dag thams cad yongs su thar par bya'o zhes/ de la byang chub sems dpa' snying rje chen pos yongs su rgyas pa'i sems dang ldan pas/
160a1(phal chen): sems can gyi khams 'khor ba'i 'dam du bying ba mthong nas/ sems can de dag la snying brtse ba chen po skyes pa/ phan cher gdags pa'i sems rab tu bskyed pa
160a2(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi don chen po bya bar dga' ba/ sems can mang po rab tu dgrol bar dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bsngo ba/ yongs su bsngo ba chen po la zhugs pa dang / 'das pa dang
160a3(phal chen): ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi yongs su bsngo ba la rab tu zhugs pa/ bsngo ba chen po'i mdos sems can thams cad la dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yongs
160a4(phal chen): su bsngo ba/ sems can thams cad shin tu rnam par dag par bya bar sems pa/ sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba kun thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mthar thug par yongs su bsngo ba
160a5(phal chen): de/ sems 'di lta bu dang ldan par 'gyur te/ sems can thams cad bla na med pa'i ye shes kyi rgyal srid la rab tu gzhag pa'i phyir bdag spyod de/ bdag ni bdag 'ba' zhig yongs su
160a6(phal chen): dgrol ba la mngon par zhugs pa ma yin gyis/ bdag gis sems can 'di dag kun thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems rab tu snang bas 'khor ba'i dgon pa brgal dka' ba nas gdon par bya'o// /
160a7(phal chen): g.yang sa chen po nas blang bar bya'o// gnod pa thams cad las yongs su dgrol bar bya'o// 'khor ba'i rgyud las rab tu bsgral bar bya'o// bdag nyid kyis sems can thams cad kyi
160b1(phal chen): sdug bsngal gyi phung po blang bar spro bar bya'o/ / bdag gis sems can de dag thams cad 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal chen po'i sa'i 'og nas drang bar bya'o// 'jig rten gyi khams kyi mthar thug
160b2(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi ngan song kun gyi sdug bsngal thams cad blangs te/ nyams su myong bar bya ba la bdag gis spro bar bya'o// bdag gis sems can thams cad dge ba'i rtsa ba las mi spang bar
160b3(phal chen): bya'o/ / sems can thams cad yongs su dgrol ba'i phyir/ bdag ngan song gcig na phyi ma'i mthar thug pa'i bskal par gnas par spro bar bya'o// ngan song gcig tu ji lta ba de bzhin du 'jig
160b4(phal chen): rten gyi khams thams cad du gtogs pa'i ngan song thams cad du gnas par spro bar bya'o/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kyi hud sems can 'di dag thams cad sdug bsngal gyi gnas su lhung ba bas ni bdag
160b5(phal chen): gcig spu sdug bsngal myong yang bla'i/ bdag gis der bdag nyid gtar bcugs ste/ sems can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi dgon pa nas 'gro ba
160b6(phal chen): thams cad blus te/ bdag gis sems can thams cad kyi don du sdug bsngal tshor ba'i phung po 'di dag thams cad bdag gis lus 'dis myong bar bya'o// bdag gis ni sems can rnams kyi
160b7(phal chen): gzha' bden par smra ba dang / yid ches shing mi slu bar spro bar bya'i// bdag la ni sems can thams cad kyis ma yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ 'gro ba thams cad yongs su dgrol
161a1(phal chen): ba'i phyir/ bdag gis thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems can thams cad la dmigs pa skye ste/ bdag nyid 'dod pa'i phyir ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
161a2(phal chen): byang chub tu ma zhugs so/ / 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga la dga' zhing spyod pa'i phyir yang ma yin no// 'dod pa'i yul la bsnyen pa'i phyir yang ma yin no// 'dod pa'i khams su gtogs
161a3(phal chen): pa'i dga' ba mang po gzhan blang ba'i phyir yang byang chub kyi spyod pa la mi spyod do/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'jig rten gyi dga' ba 'di dag thams cad ni dgra yin no// 'dod pa la brten pa 'di
161a4(phal chen): ni bdud kyi yul lo/ / 'dod pa la brten pa de ni blo ngan pas bstan pa'i lam mo// sangs rgyas thams cad kyis sman pa'i yul lo// de dag la brten pa de las sdug bsngal thams cad
161a5(phal chen): 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ / de las sems can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten 'di dag thams cad kyang 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de las sems can rnams
161a6(phal chen): 'thab pa dang / mtshang 'dru ba dang / rtsod pa dang / gnad la 'bebs pa dang / 'khrug pa dang / kun tu 'khrug pa rnams kyang rab tu 'byung ngo // sems can 'di dag ni 'dod pa la brten
161a7(phal chen): pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams las ring du gyur pa ste/ 'dod pa de dag ni mtho ris su skye ba la yang bar du gcod na/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub lta la
161b1(phal chen): spos kyang ci dgos te/ sems can thams cad kyi bde ba dang dga' ba thams cad kyi yang bar du 'gyur ro// de ltar bdag gis 'don pa ni ro chung ni 'chad med pa'i nyes pa can du mthong
161b2(phal chen): na/ cing yang de dag spyod pa'i phyir 'jug gam/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bdag ni don 'di dag gi phyir bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu zhugs pa ma yin no// 'dod pa
161b3(phal chen): la dga' ba'i phyir yang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la mi spyod de/ de bas na sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde bar zhugs pa'i sems bskyed de/ bdag ni 'di ltar
161b4(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi don gyi phyir/ de dag nyid kyi smon lam yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / bsngo zhing bsgrub pa'i phyir don de la zhugs pa ste/ de bas na bdag gis sa
161b5(phal chen): can sdug bsngal gyi zhags pas bcings la thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi zhags pa bcad de/ sdug bsngal thams cad las yongs su dgrol bar bya'o// sdug bsngal gyi rgyud
161b6(phal chen): las rnam par bzlog par bya'o/ / bdag gis ji lta ji ltar sems can 'di dag thams cad shin tu bde ba dang / phan par 'gyur ba'i bde ba dang / tshor ba med pa'i bde ba dang /
161b7(phal chen): zhi ba'i bde ba dang / mi gnas pa'i bde ba dang / mi g.yo ba'i bde ba dang / tshad med pa'i bde ba dang / ma nyams pa'i bde ba dang / mi 'gag pa'i bde ba dang / thams cad mkhyen
162a1(phal chen): pa nyid kyi bde ba rab tu thob par 'gyur ba de lta de ltar dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yongs su bsngo bar bya'o/ / bdag pa lo sbyar ba dang / bdug mgon po dang / bdag ma na
162a2(phal chen): 'dzin pa dang / bdag lam bde ba ston pa dang / bdag khom pa rnyed pa dang / bdag thabs la mkhas pa dang / bdag don shes pa dang / bdag 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho la thams cad mkhyen
162a3(phal chen): ba'i gru bo che'i mnyan par gyur pa dang / bdag yongs su bsngo ba la mkhas pa dang / bdag pha rol ston pas dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag ji lta ji ltar sems can rnams kyi skyabs su 'gyur ba dang /
162a4(phal chen): 'khor bar gyur pa rnams yongs su rgal bar 'gyur ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par 'gyur ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du bsgribs pa med par 'gyur ba dang
162a5(phal chen): bdud kyi yul rnams la mi gnas par 'gyur ba dang / sdig pa mi dge ba'i grogs po thams cad yongs su spong bar 'gyur ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen byang chub sems dpa' thams cad
162a6(phal chen): la brten par 'gyur ba dang / las rnam par dag pa la kha na ma tho ba med par 'gyur ba dang / spyad pa chen po'i smon lam rnams yang dag par bsgrub par 'gyur ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba
162a7(phal chen): thams cad khong du chud par 'gyur ba de lta de ltar yongs su bsngo'o/ / de la byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yongs su bsngo ba na/ sems 'di snyam du bskyed de/ kye ma
162b1(phal chen): gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi mas snang bar bya ba'i phyir/ gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams na sems can ji snyed pa de snyed kyi nyi ma ni mi 'char gyi/ gling bzhi'i 'jig rten snang bar bya ba'i phyi
162b2(phal chen): nyi ma 'di nyid gcig pu 'char te/ sems can gling bzhir gtogs pa de dag rang rang gi lus las kyang snang ba gang gis/ de dag gis nyi ma'i grangs shes par 'gyur ba 'am
162b3(phal chen): rang gi don bsgrub par 'gyur ba 'am/ lo tog yongs su smin par 'gyur ba 'am/ nyin cig nyin cig cing bza' shing gi ra ba na/ grong khyer dag tu dga' ba dang rtse ba'i longs spyod myong
162b4(phal chen): bar 'gyur ba 'am/ phyogs snang bar 'gyur ba 'am/ grong dang / grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / pho brang 'khor dang / rgyal ba'i gnas dag tu 'gro ba dang 'ong bar bya ba dang
162b5(phal chen): spyod pa'i don sbyar bar bya ba'i snang ba mi 'byung ste/ sems can de dag rang rang gi lus la yang 'od gang gis de dag bsgrub pa'i 'od de lta bu mi gtong ste/ 'di ltar lha'i bu nyi ma'i dkyil
162b6(phal chen): 'khor gcig pu gnyis su med pa de ni/ gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams su sems can rnams la snang bar bya ba'i phyir 'char zhing rab tu 'byung ngo // de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'
